							Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey = TOTDKeyToFocus;
							FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, _IsFocus);
							break;
						}
						TOTDKeyToFocus -= 1;
					}
				}
			} else {
				FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, _IsFocus);
			}
		}
	} else {
		if (TOTD_Frames.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey)) {
			if (_IsFocus && !TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey].Visible) {
				if (TOTD_Frames.count >= C_MonthlyPerLine) {
					declare Integer TOTDKeyToFocus = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey;
					while (TOTDKeyToFocus >= 0) {
						if (TOTD_Frames[TOTDKeyToFocus].Visible) {
							Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey = TOTDKeyToFocus;
							FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, _IsFocus);
							break;
						}
						TOTDKeyToFocus -= 1;
					}
				}
			} else {
				FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, _IsFocus);
			}
		}
	}
}

Void UnfocusLastMonthly(CMlScript _This, Boolean _IsRoyal) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	if (_IsRoyal) {
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollRoyalFocus != Null) {
			FocusMonthly(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollRoyalFocus, False, _IsRoyal);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollRoyalFocus = Null;
		}
	} else {
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollMonthlyFocus != Null) {
			FocusMonthly(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollMonthlyFocus, False, _IsRoyal);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollMonthlyFocus = Null;
		}
	}
}

Void UnfocusLastMonthlies(CMlScript _This) {
	UnfocusLastMonthly(_This, False);
	UnfocusLastMonthly(_This, True);
}

Void FocusMonthlyByMouse(CMlScript _This, CMlFrame _Frame_TOTD, Boolean _IsRoyal) {
	if (_Frame_TOTD != Null) {
		if (_Frame_TOTD.DataAttributeExists("key") && _Frame_TOTD.Parent != Null) {
			declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
			UnfocusLastMonthly(_This, _IsRoyal);
			if (_IsRoyal) {
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey = TL::ToInteger(_Frame_TOTD.DataAttributeGet("key"));
			} else {
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey = TL::ToInteger(_Frame_TOTD.DataAttributeGet("key"));
			}
			assert(_Frame_TOTD.Parent.HasClass(Scroll::C_Class_Element), "We are not pointing to the correct frame anymore");
			declare Integer MonthlyScrollKey for _Frame_TOTD.Parent;
			Scroll::SetFocusedElementKey(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD, MonthlyScrollKey, True, True);
		}
	}
}

Void FocusMonthlyByInput(CMlScript _This, CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction _Input, CMlFrame _Frame_Element, Boolean _IsRoyal) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare CMlControl[] TOTD_Frames = GetLineControls(_Frame_Element);
	switch (_Input) {
		case CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Right : {
			if (_IsRoyal) {
				if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey + 1 < C_MonthlyPerLine) {
					if (TOTD_Frames.count >= C_MonthlyPerLine && TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey + 1].Visible) {
						if (TOTD_Frames.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey)) FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, False);
						Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey + 1;
						FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, True);
					}
				}
			} else {
				if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey + 1 < C_MonthlyPerLine) {
					if (TOTD_Frames.count >= C_MonthlyPerLine && TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey + 1].Visible) {
						if (TOTD_Frames.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey)) FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, False);
						Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey + 1;
						FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, True);
					}
				}
			}
		}
		case CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Left : {
			if (_IsRoyal) {
				if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey - 1 >= 0) {
					if (TOTD_Frames.count >= C_MonthlyPerLine && TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey - 1].Visible) {
						if (TOTD_Frames.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey)) FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, False);
						Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey - 1;
						FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, True);
					}
				} else {
					Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
				}
			} else {
				if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey - 1 >= 0) {
					if (TOTD_Frames.count >= C_MonthlyPerLine && TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey - 1].Visible) {
						if (TOTD_Frames.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey)) FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, False);
						Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey - 1;
						FocusTOTD(_This, TOTD_Frames[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey] as CMlFrame, True);
					}
				} else {
					Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

Void ResetMyTracks(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks = [];
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks = [];
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentPath = "";
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentParentPath = "";
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.FocusParentFolder = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LastFolderSelected_Keys.clear();
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetLocalTracks = Task::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetLocalTracks);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetOnlineTracks = Task::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetOnlineTracks);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus = Task::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task = Task::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Name = "";
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.FileName = "";
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Uid = "";
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task = Task::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Name = "";
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Uid = "";
}

Void ResetFavorites(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.IsLoadingTracks = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.RemoveTrack.Name = "";
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.RemoveTrack.Uid = "";
}

Void ResetOfficial(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	UnfocusLastOfficialCampaign(_This);
	UnfocusLastMonthlies(_This);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingTracks = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns = [];
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingCampaigns = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey = 0;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollCampaignFocus = Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentCampaign = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies = [];
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingMonthly = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey = 0;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollMonthlyFocus = Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.ScrollMonthlyOffset = 0;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageMonthly = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentMonthly = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals = [];
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingRoyal = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey = 0;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollRoyalFocus = Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.ScrollRoyalOffset = 0;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageRoyal = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentRoyal = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentMonthDays.clear();
}

Void ResetClubs(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.Clubs = [];
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.IsLoadingClubs = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClub = ClubStruct::LibStructuresClub_K_Club {};
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.IsLoadingCampaigns = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns = [];
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.FocusParentClub = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClubKey = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.IsLoadingCampaignTracks = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.FocusParentCampaign = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaignKey = -1;
}

Void ResetTracksFavoriteStatus(CMlScript _This, Boolean _ResetKnownedFavorites) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request = Http::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CheckRequestTime = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.LastAddOrRemoveRequestTime = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.FirstHeartIconDisplay = False;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.UidsToCheck.clear();
	if (_ResetKnownedFavorites)	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.KnownedFavoritesTracksUids.clear();
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CurrentTrackUid = "";
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CurrentTrackName = "";
}

Void Reset(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	switch (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex) {
		case C_TabIndex_None: {
			ResetMyTracks(_This);
			ResetFavorites(_This);
			ResetOfficial(_This);
			ResetClubs(_This);
		}
		case C_TabIndex_MyTracks: {
			ResetFavorites(_This);
			ResetOfficial(_This);
			ResetClubs(_This);
		}
		case C_TabIndex_Favorites: {
			ResetMyTracks(_This);
			ResetOfficial(_This);
			ResetClubs(_This);
		}
		case C_TabIndex_Official: {
			ResetMyTracks(_This);
			ResetFavorites(_This);
			ResetClubs(_This);
		}
		case C_TabIndex_Clubs: {
			ResetMyTracks(_This);
			ResetFavorites(_This);
			ResetOfficial(_This);
		}
	}
	ResetTracksFavoriteStatus(_This, False);
}

Void EnableOption(CMlFrame _Button, Boolean _Enable) {
	if (_Button == Null) return;
	_Button.Visible = _Enable;
	Navigation::Lock(_Button, !_Enable);
}

Void CheckButtonSelectAllTracks(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare Boolean AllTracksChecked = True;
	// Manual limit set to avoid checking too much tracks
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.count > C_MaxSelectedTracksCountCheck || Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks.count > C_MaxSelectedTracksCountCheck) {
		AllTracksChecked = False;
	} else {
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks) {
			declare Integer FoldersNb = 0;
			foreach (Track in Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks) {
				if (Track.SubFolder == "" && !Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks.existskey(Track.TrackInfo.Uid)) {
					AllTracksChecked = False;
					break;
				} else if (Track.SubFolder != "") {
					FoldersNb += 1;
				}
			}
			if (FoldersNb == Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.count) {
				AllTracksChecked = False;
			}
		} else {
			// If there is more tracks displayed than in the selected array, no need to check
			if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks.count > Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks.count) {
				AllTracksChecked = False;
			} else {
				foreach (Track in Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks) {
					if (!Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks.existskey(Track.Uid)) {
						AllTracksChecked = False;
						break;
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	Checkbox::Check(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll, AllTracksChecked);
}

Void ShowOptions(CMlScript _This, Boolean _Show) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Options.Visible = _Show;
	// SelectAll button unavailable when tracks API uses an offset (for now only Favorites, later in Online Tracks too)
	EnableOption(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll, _Show && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex != C_TabIndex_Favorites);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.ButtonIcon_SelectAll.Visible = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.Visible;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SpaceDisk.Visible = _Show && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks && Platform::IsFromFirstParty(System);
	EnableOption(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Flatten, _Show && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks && Platform::IsPC(System));
	EnableOption(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Refresh, _Show && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks && Platform::IsPC(System));
	EnableOption(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_OpenExplorer, _Show && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks && Platform::IsPC(System));
	EnableOption(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Sort, _Show && (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks || Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Favorites));
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.ButtonIcon_Sort.Visible = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Sort.Visible;
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.Visible) {
		declare CMlLabel Label_SelectAll = Checkbox::GetLabel(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll);
		declare Real LabelWidth = ML::Min(Label_SelectAll.ComputeWidth(Label_SelectAll.Value), Checkbox::GetLabelSize(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll).X);
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Flatten.Visible) {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X = -27.;
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.ButtonIcon_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X - LabelWidth + 2.5;
		} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SpaceDisk.Visible) {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X = -49.;
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.ButtonIcon_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X - LabelWidth + 2.5;
		} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Sort.Visible) {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X = -1.;
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.ButtonIcon_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X - LabelWidth + 2.5;
		} else {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X = 27.5;
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.ButtonIcon_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.RelativePosition_V3.X + 17.;
		}
	}
}

Void EnableMultiSelect(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	UpdateAddTracksButtonVisibility(_This);
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_SubTitle.Value = C_Text_SubTitlePlural;
	} else {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_SubTitle.Value = C_Text_SubTitleSingular;
	}
}

// Navigation between tabs (My Tracks, Favorites, Official and Clubs) and tabs sections
Void GoToTabAndSection(CMlScript _This, Integer _TabIndex, Integer _Section) {
	if (!C_TabNames.existskey(_TabIndex)) return;
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex = _TabIndex;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection = _Section;
	UserStore::SetTrackBrowser_Tab(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex);
	Reset(_This);
	if (NavigationTabs::GetCurrentTab(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs) != Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex) {
		NavigationTabs::UpdateCurrentTab(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex, False);
	}

	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MyTracks.Hide();
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Official.Hide();
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Clubs.Hide();
	ShowOptions(_This, False);
	Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, 0);
	Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs, 0);
	// We don't want to send a Focus Event to the Official campaigns and Monthlies scrolls because it compromises the behaviour of the ColumnFocusKey variable
	Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Official_Campaigns, 0, False);
	Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD, 0, False);
	SetSectionTitle(_This, "");
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_Error.Value = "";
	declare Text ButtonBack_UpTargetId = "";
	declare Text ButtonBack_RightTargetId = "";
	UpdateControllerInfos(_This);

	switch (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex) {
		case C_TabIndex_MyTracks: {
			switch (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection) {
				case C_Section_None: {
					SetSectionTitle(_This, C_Text_Tracks);
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MyTracks.Show();
					Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LastButtonFocused);
					ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LastButtonFocused.ControlId;
				}
				case C_Section_LocalTracks: {
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MyTracks.Hide();
					ShowOptions(_This, True);
					if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.NeedRefresh) {
						DataFileMgr.Map_RefreshFromDisk();
						Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.NeedRefresh = False;
					}
					UpdateLocalTracks(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentPath);
					ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks.ControlId;
					ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
				}
				case C_Section_OnlineTracks: {
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MyTracks.Hide();
					ShowOptions(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect);
					UpdateOnlineTracks(_This);
					ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks.ControlId;
					ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
				}
			}
		}
		case C_TabIndex_Favorites: {
			SetSectionTitle(_This, C_Text_FavoriteTracks);
			ShowOptions(_This, True);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.IsLoadingTracks = True;
			UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
			ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks.ControlId;
			ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
			Scroll::TriggerPagerUpdate(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks);
		}
		case C_TabIndex_Official: {
			switch (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection) {
				case C_Section_None: {
					SetSectionTitle(_This, C_Text_Official);
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Official.Show();
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_OfficialButtons.Show();
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_DayTOTD.SetText(""^Tools::GetMonthDay());
					if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastButtonFocused == Null || Navigation::IsLocked(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastButtonFocused)) {
						Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastButtonFocused = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_OfficialCampaigns;
					}
					Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastButtonFocused);
					ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastButtonFocused.ControlId;
				}
				case C_Section_OfficialCampaigns: {
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Official.Show();
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_OfficialButtons.Hide();
					SetSectionTitle(_This, C_Text_OfficialCampaigns);
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingCampaigns = True;
					UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
					CampaignStore::Action_LoadLiveQuarterlyCampaign(_This, CampaignAPI::C_CachePreload_CampaignOfficial);
					ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Official_Campaigns.ControlId;
					ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
				}
				case C_Section_SelectedOfficialCampaign: {
					if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey].existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey)) {
						declare Text CampaignName = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey].Name;
						SetSectionTitle(_This, TL::Compose(C_Text_SelectedCampaign, CampaignName));
						UpdateOfficialTracks(_This);
						ShowOptions(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect);
						ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks.ControlId;
						ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
					}
				}
				case C_Section_Monthly: {
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Official.Show();
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_OfficialButtons.Hide();
					SetSectionTitle(_This, C_Text_TOTD);
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingMonthly = True;
					UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageMonthly = -1; // To trigger the pager update
					ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD.ControlId;
					ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
				}
				case C_Section_SelectedMonthly: {
					if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey].existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey)) {
						declare Text MonthlyName = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey].MonthName;
						SetSectionTitle(_This, TL::Compose(C_Text_SelectedTOTD, MonthlyName));
						UpdateOfficialTracks(_This);
						ShowOptions(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect);
						ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks.ControlId;
						ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
					}
				}
				case C_Section_Royal: {
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Official.Show();
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_OfficialButtons.Hide();
					SetSectionTitle(_This, C_Text_Royal);
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingRoyal = True;
					UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageRoyal = -1; // To trigger the pager update
					ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD.ControlId;
					ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
				}
				case C_Section_SelectedRoyal: {
					if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey].existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey)) {
						declare Text RoyalName = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey].MonthName;
						SetSectionTitle(_This, TL::Compose(C_Text_SelectedRoyal, RoyalName));
						UpdateOfficialTracks(_This);
						ShowOptions(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect);
						ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks.ControlId;
						ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
					}
				}
			}
		}
		case C_TabIndex_Clubs: {
			switch (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection) {
				case C_Section_None: {
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Clubs.Show();
					SetSectionTitle(_This, C_Text_MyClubsTracks);
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.IsLoadingClubs = True;
					UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
					ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs.ControlId;
					ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
					Scroll::TriggerPagerUpdate(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs);
				}
				case C_Section_SelectedClub: {
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Clubs.Show();
					SetSectionTitle(_This, TL::Compose(C_Text_SelectedClub, "$<"^Tools::FormatValue(FilterProfanities(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClub.Name))^"$>"));
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.IsLoadingCampaigns = True;
					UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
					ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs.ControlId;
					ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
					Scroll::TriggerPagerUpdate(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs);
				}
				case C_Section_SelectedClubCampaign: {
					if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaignKey)) {
						declare Integer SelectedCampaignId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaignKey].Id;
						UpdateClubCampaignTracks(_This, SelectedCampaignId);
						ShowOptions(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect);
						ButtonBack_UpTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks.ControlId;
						ButtonBack_RightTargetId = ButtonBack_UpTargetId;
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	EnableMultiSelect(_This);
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_AddTracks.Visible) {
		ButtonBack_RightTargetId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_AddTracks.ControlId;
	}
	Navigation::ChangeControlTargets(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back, ["up", "right"], [ButtonBack_UpTargetId, ButtonBack_RightTargetId]);
}

Void GoToTab(CMlScript _This, Integer _TabIndex) {
	return GoToTabAndSection(_This, _TabIndex, C_Section_None);
}

Void GoToSection(CMlScript _This, Integer _Section) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	return GoToTabAndSection(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex, _Section);
}

Void Refresh(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_Error.Value = "";
	switch (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection) {
		case C_Section_None: {
			if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Favorites) {
				Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, 0);
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.IsLoadingTracks = True;
				UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
				Scroll::TriggerPagerUpdate(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks);
			}
		}
		case C_Section_LocalTracks: {
			DataFileMgr.Map_RefreshFromDisk();
			UpdateLocalTracks(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentPath);
		}
	}
}

// Update the navigation tabs depending on browser setttings
Void UpdateNavigationTabs(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare Text[Integer] TabNames = C_TabNames;

	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.ShowOnlyMyLocalTracks) {
		TabNames = [C_TabIndex_MyTracks => C_TabNames[C_TabIndex_MyTracks]];
	}

	if (!Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CanViewUGC) {
		TabNames.removekey(C_TabIndex_Favorites);
		TabNames.removekey(C_TabIndex_Clubs);
	}

	NavigationTabs::SetTabs(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs, TabNames, False);
	NavigationTabs::RedrawNavigationTabs(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs, False);
}

Void LockScroll(CMlFrame _Frame_Scroll, Boolean _Lock) {
	Scroll::LockNavigation(_Frame_Scroll, _Lock);
	Navigation::Lock(_Frame_Scroll, _Lock);
}

Void RetrievePersistentTrackBrowser(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare UserStore::K_TrackBrowserInfos CurrentBrowser = UserStore::GetPersistentTrackBrowserInfos();

	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex = CurrentBrowser.CurrentTabIndex;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsFlatten = CurrentBrowser.IsFlatten;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingByNameElseByDate = CurrentBrowser.IsSortingByNameElseByDate;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingFromAscendingOrder = CurrentBrowser.IsSortingFromAscendingOrder;
}

Void RetrievePreviousTrackBrowser(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentSection for LocalUser = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentSection;
	// Local tracks
	declare Text Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPath for LocalUser = "";
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentPath = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPath;
	// Official campaigns
	declare K_OfficialCampaign[][Integer] Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaigns for LocalUser = [];
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaignLineSelectedKey for LocalUser = -1;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaignColumnFocusKey for LocalUser = 0;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaigns;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaignLineSelectedKey;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaignColumnFocusKey;
	// Monthly campaigns
	declare K_MonthlyCampaign[][Integer] Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Monthlies for LocalUser = [];
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_MonthlyColumnFocusKey for LocalUser = 0;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_ScrollMonthlyOffset for LocalUser = 0;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPageMonthly for LocalUser = -1;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_MonthlyLineSelectedKey for LocalUser = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Monthlies;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_MonthlyColumnFocusKey;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.ScrollMonthlyOffset = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_ScrollMonthlyOffset;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageMonthly = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPageMonthly;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_MonthlyLineSelectedKey;
	// Royal campaigns
	declare K_MonthlyCampaign[][Integer] Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Royals for LocalUser = [];
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_RoyalColumnFocusKey for LocalUser = 0;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_ScrollRoyalOffset for LocalUser = 0;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPageRoyal for LocalUser = -1;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_RoyalLineSelectedKey for LocalUser = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Royals;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_RoyalColumnFocusKey;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.ScrollRoyalOffset = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_ScrollRoyalOffset;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageRoyal = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPageRoyal;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_RoyalLineSelectedKey;
	// Club campaigns
	declare ClubStruct::LibStructuresClub_K_Club[Integer] Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Clubs for LocalUser = [];
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubKey for LocalUser = -1;
	declare ClubStruct::LibStructuresClub_K_Club Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClub for LocalUser = ClubStruct::LibStructuresClub_K_Club {};
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubCampaignKey for LocalUser = -1;
	declare CampaignStruct::LibCampaignStruct_K_Campaign[Integer] Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubCampaigns for LocalUser = [];
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.Clubs = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Clubs;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClubKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubKey;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClub = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClub;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaignKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubCampaignKey;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubCampaigns;
}

Void SavePreviousTrackBrowser(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentSection for LocalUser = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentSection = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection;
	// Local tracks
	declare Text Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPath for LocalUser = "";
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPath = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentPath;
	// Official campaigns
	declare K_OfficialCampaign[][Integer] Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaigns for LocalUser = [];
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaignLineSelectedKey for LocalUser = -1;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaignColumnFocusKey for LocalUser = 0;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaigns = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaignLineSelectedKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_OfficialCampaignColumnFocusKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey;
	// Monthly campaigns
	declare K_MonthlyCampaign[][Integer] Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Monthlies for LocalUser = [];
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_MonthlyColumnFocusKey for LocalUser = 0;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_ScrollMonthlyOffset for LocalUser = 0;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPageMonthly for LocalUser = -1;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_MonthlyLineSelectedKey for LocalUser = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Monthlies = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_MonthlyColumnFocusKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_ScrollMonthlyOffset = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.ScrollMonthlyOffset;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPageMonthly = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageMonthly;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_MonthlyLineSelectedKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey;
	// Royal campaigns
	declare K_MonthlyCampaign[][Integer] Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Royals for LocalUser = [];
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_RoyalColumnFocusKey for LocalUser = 0;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_ScrollRoyalOffset for LocalUser = 0;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPageRoyal for LocalUser = -1;
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_RoyalLineSelectedKey for LocalUser = -1;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Royals = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_RoyalColumnFocusKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_ScrollRoyalOffset = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.ScrollRoyalOffset;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_CurrentPageRoyal = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageRoyal;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_RoyalLineSelectedKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey;
	// Club campaigns
	declare ClubStruct::LibStructuresClub_K_Club[Integer] Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Clubs for LocalUser = [];
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubKey for LocalUser = -1;
	declare ClubStruct::LibStructuresClub_K_Club Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClub for LocalUser = ClubStruct::LibStructuresClub_K_Club {};
	declare Integer Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubCampaignKey for LocalUser = -1;
	declare CampaignStruct::LibCampaignStruct_K_Campaign[Integer] Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubCampaigns for LocalUser = [];
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_Clubs = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.Clubs;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClubKey;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClub = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClub;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubCampaignKey = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaignKey ;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_SelectedClubCampaigns = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns;
}

Boolean IsSectionCorrespondingToTab(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	return C_TabSectionRelationship.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex) && C_TabSectionRelationship[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex].exists(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection);
}

Boolean IsSectionDisplayPossible(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare Boolean IsSectionDisplayPossible = False;
	switch (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection) {
		case C_Section_OfficialCampaigns, C_Section_SelectedOfficialCampaign: {
			IsSectionDisplayPossible = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns.count > 0;
		}
		case C_Section_Monthly, C_Section_SelectedMonthly: {
			IsSectionDisplayPossible = (
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CanViewUGC &&
				(
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Filters.FilterByMapType.count == 0 ||
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Filters.FilterByMapType.exists(Const::C_MapType_Race_NoConcat)
				) &&
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies.count > 0
			);
		}
		case C_Section_Royal, C_Section_SelectedRoyal: {
			IsSectionDisplayPossible = (
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CanViewUGC &&
				(
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Filters.FilterByMapType.count == 0 ||
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Filters.FilterByMapType.exists(Const::C_MapType_Royal_NoConcat)
				) &&
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals.count > 0
			);
		}
		case C_Section_SelectedClub, C_Section_SelectedClubCampaign: {
			IsSectionDisplayPossible = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.Clubs.count > 0 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns.count > 0;
		}
		default: IsSectionDisplayPossible = True;
	}
	return IsSectionDisplayPossible;
}

Void LockBrowser(CMlScript _This, Boolean _Lock) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Navigation::EnableGroup(_This, C_NavGroupName, !_Lock);
	Navigation::EnableGroup(_This, C_NavGroupGlobal, !_Lock);
	NavigationTabs::LockTabs(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs, _Lock);
	LockScroll(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, _Lock);
}

Void UpdateRoyalVictoriesDisplay(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare UserStore::K_MatchmakingInfo RoyalMatchmakingInfo = UserStore::GetMatchmakingInfos(MatchmakingStruct::C_Mode_Royal);
	PlayerRoyalVictories::SetDivisions(_This, RoyalMatchmakingInfo.Divisions);
	PlayerRoyalVictories::UpdatePlayerRoyalVictories(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_RoyalVictory, RoyalMatchmakingInfo.PlayerProgression.CurrentDivision, RoyalMatchmakingInfo.PlayerProgression.CurrentProgression);
}

CManiaApp Private_GetParentApp(CMlScript _This) {
	switchtype (_This as Context) {
		case CMlScriptIngame: {
			return Context.ParentApp;
		}
		case CManiaAppTitleLayer: {
			return Context.ParentApp;
		}
	}

	return Null;
}

Void Private_UpateTOTDAndRoyalAccess(CMlScript _This, Boolean _UpdateTabAndSection) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;

	// Update TOTD button visibility
	if (
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CanViewUGC && (
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Filters.FilterByMapType.count == 0 ||
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Filters.FilterByMapType.exists(Const::C_MapType_Race_NoConcat)
		)
	) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_DayTOTD.Show();
		Button::ShowAndUnlock(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_TOTD);
	}	else {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_DayTOTD.Hide();
		Button::HideAndLock(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_TOTD);
	}

	// Update Royal button visibility
	if (
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CanViewUGC && (
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Filters.FilterByMapType.count == 0 ||
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Filters.FilterByMapType.exists(Const::C_MapType_Royal_NoConcat)
		)
	) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_RoyalVictory.Show();
		Button::ShowAndUnlock(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Royal);
		UpdateRoyalVictoriesDisplay(_This);
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_TOTD.Visible) Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Royal.RelativePosition_V3.X = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.ManialinkProps.Pos_ThirdHorizontalButton.X;
		else Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Royal.RelativePosition_V3.X = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.ManialinkProps.Pos_SecondHorizontalButton.X;
	}	else {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_RoyalVictory.Hide();
		Button::HideAndLock(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Royal);
	}

	// Force an update of the section to focus the right element if the TOTD and Royal buttons are hidden and locked
	if (
		_UpdateTabAndSection &&
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Official && (
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_None ||
			!IsSectionDisplayPossible(_This)
		)
	) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection = C_Section_None;
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastButtonFocused = Null;
		GoToTabAndSection(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection);
	}
}

Void Display(CMlScript _This, Boolean _Visible, Boolean _SendExitEvent) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	// Don't re show or hide browser if is already in the right display
	if ((_Visible && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.Visible) || (!_Visible && !Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.Visible)) return;

	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.Visible = _Visible;
	LockBrowser(_This, !_Visible);

	if (_Visible) {
		// Automatic local tracks refresh on browser opening (mandatory for console which do not have a refresh button)
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.NeedRefresh = True;

		// If game is offline, restrain track browser to local tracks
		if (UserStore::IsOfflineMode()) {
			SetShowOnlyMyLocalTracks(_This, True);
		} else {
			declare UserStore::K_MatchmakingInfo RoyalMatchmakingInfo = UserStore::GetMatchmakingInfos(MatchmakingStruct::C_Mode_Royal);
			if (RoyalMatchmakingInfo.Divisions.count <= 0) { //< Try to load matchmaking infos again if not loaded correctly
				UserStore::Action_LoadMatchmakingInfos(_This, LocalUser.WebServicesUserId);
			}
		}
		UpdateNavigationTabs(_This);

		// Retrieve sort settings and last open tab (persistent infos)
		RetrievePersistentTrackBrowser(_This);
		// Retrieve last section and data to re-open it (not persistent infos)
		RetrievePreviousTrackBrowser(_This);

		Private_UpateTOTDAndRoyalAccess(_This, False);

		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.ShowOnlyMyLocalTracks) {
			GoToTabAndSection(_This, C_TabIndex_MyTracks, C_Section_LocalTracks);
		} else if (
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.OpenOnLastTab &&
			NavigationTabs::IsAvailableTab(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex)
		) {
			// Security in case we try to open a sub section and we do not have the mandatory informations to display it
			if (!IsSectionCorrespondingToTab(_This) || !IsSectionDisplayPossible(_This)) {
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection = C_Section_None;
			}
			GoToTabAndSection(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection);
		} else if (NavigationTabs::IsAvailableTab(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.ChosenOpeningTab)) {
			GoToTab(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.ChosenOpeningTab);
		} else {
			GoToTab(_This, C_TabIndex_MyTracks);
		}

		Checkbox::Check(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Flatten, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsFlatten);
		Checkbox::Check(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SortOption1, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingByNameElseByDate);
		Checkbox::Check(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SortOption2, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingFromAscendingOrder);

		// Check that the user can view UGC
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.UGCPrivilegeCheck = Privileges::Check_DestroyAndCreate(
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.UGCPrivilegeCheck,
			PrivilegeMgr,
			MainUser::GetMainUserId(),
			CPrivilegeMgr::EPrivilege::UseUserCreatedContent
		);

		// Text to speech context
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TTSContextIdent_Tabs = Private_GetParentApp(_This).TTS_Context_Enter(TextToSpeech::C_ContextLevel_Component);
		Private_GetParentApp(_This).TTS_Context_Change(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TTSContextIdent_Tabs, NavigationTabs::GetCurrentTabLabel(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs));
		Private_GetParentApp(_This).TTS_Context_Read(TextToSpeech::C_ContextLevel_Component);
	} else {
		Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
		LockScroll(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, True);
		LockScroll(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs, True);
		LockScroll(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Official_Campaigns, True);
		LockScroll(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD, True);
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks.clear();
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect) {
			ExpendableButton::SetText(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_AddTracks, C_Text_AddTracks);
		}
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Official) {
			UnfocusLastOfficialCampaign(_This);
			UnfocusLastMonthlies(_This);
		}
		ResetTracksFavoriteStatus(_This, True);
		ControllerInfo::SetButtons([]);
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_Error.Value = "";
		SavePreviousTrackBrowser(_This);
		if (_SendExitEvent) {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.DelayedPendingEvents.add(K_Event {
				Type = C_Event_Exit
			});
		}
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.UGCPrivilegeCheck = Privileges::Check_Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.UGCPrivilegeCheck);
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TTSContextIdent_Tabs = Private_GetParentApp(_This).TTS_Context_Leave(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TTSContextIdent_Tabs);
	}
}

Void Display(CMlScript _This, Boolean _Visible) {
	Display(_This, _Visible, True);
}

Void Cancel(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	switch (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection) {
		case C_Section_None: {
			Display(_This, False);
		}
		case C_Section_LocalTracks: {
			if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentPath != "") {
				UpdateLocalTracks(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentParentPath);
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.FocusParentFolder = True;
			} else if (!Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.ShowOnlyMyLocalTracks) {
				GoToTab(_This, C_TabIndex_MyTracks);
			} else {
				Display(_This, False);
			}
		}
		case C_Section_OnlineTracks: {
			GoToTab(_This, C_TabIndex_MyTracks);
		}
		case C_Section_OfficialCampaigns: {
			UnfocusLastOfficialCampaign(_This);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey = 0;
			GoToTab(_This, C_TabIndex_Official);
		}
		case C_Section_SelectedOfficialCampaign: {
			GoToSection(_This, C_Section_OfficialCampaigns);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentCampaign = True;
		}
		case C_Section_Monthly: {
			UnfocusLastMonthly(_This, False);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey = 0;
			GoToTab(_This, C_TabIndex_Official);
		}
		case C_Section_SelectedMonthly: {
			GoToSection(_This, C_Section_Monthly);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentMonthly = True;
		}
		case C_Section_Royal: {
			UnfocusLastMonthly(_This, True);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey = 0;
			GoToTab(_This, C_TabIndex_Official);
		}
		case C_Section_SelectedRoyal: {
			GoToSection(_This, C_Section_Royal);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentRoyal = True;
		}
		case C_Section_SelectedClub: {
			GoToTab(_This, C_TabIndex_Clubs);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.FocusParentClub = True;
		}
		case C_Section_SelectedClubCampaign: {
			GoToSection(_This, C_Section_SelectedClub);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.FocusParentCampaign = True;
		}
	}
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_Error.Value = "";
}

// Checks the permission for the selected Track of the Day in the selected Monthly Campaign
K_CheckPermissionTOTD CheckPermissionTOTD(CMlScript _This, Int2 _MonthlySelectedKey, Text _TrackUid) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare Boolean HasPermission = True;
	declare Text PermissionMessage;

	if (
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies.existskey(_MonthlySelectedKey.X) &&
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies[_MonthlySelectedKey.X].existskey(_MonthlySelectedKey.Y)
	) {
		declare K_MonthlyCampaign CurrentCampaign = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies[_MonthlySelectedKey.X][_MonthlySelectedKey.Y];
		declare CampaignStruct::LibCampaignStruct_K_DailyMap SelectedDailyMap;

		declare LiveMonthlyCampaign = CampaignStore::GetLiveMonthlyCampaign();
		if (CurrentCampaign.Id == LiveMonthlyCampaign.Id) {
			foreach (DailyMap in CampaignStore::GetMonthlyCampaignFromId(CurrentCampaign.Id).DailyMaps) {
				if (DailyMap.Map.Uid == _TrackUid) {
					SelectedDailyMap = DailyMap;
					break;
				}
			}
			if (CampaignStruct::LeaderboardIsClosed(SelectedDailyMap)) {// The TOTD is not currently live
				HasPermission = UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_PlayCurrentOfficialMonthlyCampaign);
				if (!HasPermission) PermissionMessage = RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_PlayCurrentOfficialMonthlyCampaign);
			} else { // The TOTD is live
				HasPermission = UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_PlayCurrentOfficialTrackOfTheDay, SelectedDailyMap.SeasonId);
				if (!HasPermission) PermissionMessage = RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_PlayCurrentOfficialTrackOfTheDay);
			}
		} else {
			HasPermission = UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_PlayPastOfficialMonthlyCampaign);
			if (!HasPermission) PermissionMessage = RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_PlayPastOfficialMonthlyCampaign);
		}

	}
	return K_CheckPermissionTOTD {
		HasPermission = HasPermission,
		PermissionMessage = PermissionMessage
	};
}

Void SelectAllTracks(CMlScript _This, Boolean _Select) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;

	declare Text[] TrackUidsRequiringEntireCampaignAccess;
	declare Text[] TracksCouldNotBeSelected;
	declare Text PermissionMessage = "";
	if (!UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_PlayEntireOfficialQuarterlyCampaign)) {
		TrackUidsRequiringEntireCampaignAccess = RBAC::GetTrackUidsRequiringEntireCampaignAccess(CampaignStore::GetLiveQuarterlyCampaign());
	}

	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks) {	// Special behavior for Local Tracks due to sub folders
		foreach (Track in Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks) {
			if (_Select && Track.SubFolder == "") {
				if (TrackUidsRequiringEntireCampaignAccess.exists(Track.TrackInfo.Uid)) {
					if (PermissionMessage == "") {
						PermissionMessage = RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_PlayEntireOfficialQuarterlyCampaign);
					}
					if (!TracksCouldNotBeSelected.exists(Track.TrackInfo.Uid)) {
						TracksCouldNotBeSelected.add(Track.TrackInfo.Uid);
					}
				} else {
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks[Track.TrackInfo.Uid] = Track.TrackInfo;
				}
			} else {
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks.removekey(Track.TrackInfo.Uid);
			}
		}
	} else {
		foreach (Track in Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks) {
			if (_Select) {
				declare K_CheckPermissionTOTD CheckPermissionTOTD;
				if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedMonthly) {
					CheckPermissionTOTD = CheckPermissionTOTD(
						_This,
						<Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey>,
						Track.Uid
					);
				}

				if (
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedMonthly &&
					!CheckPermissionTOTD.HasPermission
				) {
					if (PermissionMessage == "") {
						PermissionMessage = CheckPermissionTOTD.PermissionMessage;
					}
					if (!TracksCouldNotBeSelected.exists(Track.Uid)) {
						TracksCouldNotBeSelected.add(Track.Uid);
					}
				} else if (TrackUidsRequiringEntireCampaignAccess.exists(Track.Uid)) {
					if (PermissionMessage == "") {
						PermissionMessage = RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_PlayEntireOfficialQuarterlyCampaign);
					}
					if (!TracksCouldNotBeSelected.exists(Track.Uid)) {
						TracksCouldNotBeSelected.add(Track.Uid);
					}
				} else {
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks[Track.Uid] = Track;
				}
			} else {
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks.removekey(Track.Uid);
			}
		}
	}

	declare CMlFrame[Integer] ElementsVisible = Scroll::GetElementsVisible(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks);
	foreach (Key => Frame_Element in ElementsVisible) {
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks) {	// Special behavior for Local Tracks due to sub folders
			if (
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.existskey(Key) &&
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[Key].SubFolder == ""
			) {
				declare Boolean IsSelected = (
					_Select && (
						TracksCouldNotBeSelected.count <= 0 ||
						!TracksCouldNotBeSelected.exists(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[Key].TrackInfo.Uid)
					)
				);
				UpdateSelectedTrack(_This, Frame_Element, IsSelected);
			}
		} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks.existskey(Key)) {
			declare Boolean IsSelected = (
				_Select && (
					TracksCouldNotBeSelected.count <= 0 ||
					!TracksCouldNotBeSelected.exists(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks[Key].Uid)
				)
			);
			UpdateSelectedTrack(_This, Frame_Element, IsSelected);
		}
	}

	if (PermissionMessage != "") {
		ClubEdition::GoToPage(_This, Router::GetCurrentRoutePath(_This), PermissionMessage);
	}
	if (TracksCouldNotBeSelected.count > 0) {
		CheckButtonSelectAllTracks(_This);
	}
}

Void Select(CMlScript _This, CMlControl _Control) {
	if (_Control == Null || Transition::IsInTransition(_This)) return;
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;

	switch (_Control.ControlId) {
		// Main menu
		case C_Id_ButtonBack: Cancel(_This);
		case C_Id_ButtonMyLocalTracks: GoToSection(_This, C_Section_LocalTracks);
		case C_Id_ButtonMyOnlineTracks: GoToSection(_This, C_Section_OnlineTracks);
		case C_Id_ButtonOfficialCampaigns: GoToSection(_This, C_Section_OfficialCampaigns);
		case C_Id_ButtonTOTD: GoToSection(_This, C_Section_Monthly);
		case C_Id_ButtonRoyal: GoToSection(_This, C_Section_Royal);
		case C_Id_ButtonAddSelectedTracks: {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.PendingEvents.add(K_Event{
				Type = C_Event_MultiSelect,
				MultiTracks = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks
			});
		}
		// Options
		case C_Id_ButtonSelectAllTracks: {
			Checkbox::Toggle(_This, _Control as CMlFrame);
			SelectAllTracks(_This, Checkbox::IsChecked(_Control as CMlFrame));
		}
		case C_Id_ButtonFlatten: {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsFlatten = Checkbox::Toggle(_This, _Control as CMlFrame);
			UserStore::SetTrackBrowser_FlattenOption(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsFlatten);
			Refresh(_This);
		}
		case C_Id_ButtonRefresh: Refresh(_This);
		case C_Id_ButtonOpenExplorer: {
			Private_GetParentApp(_This).OpenFileInExplorer("Maps\\"^Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentPath);
		}
		case C_Id_ButtonSort: PopUpMultiChoice::Open(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SortPopUp);
		case C_Id_SortOption1: {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingByNameElseByDate = Checkbox::Toggle(_This, _Control as CMlFrame);
			UserStore::SetTrackBrowser_SortOption1(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingByNameElseByDate);
		}
		case C_Id_SortOption2: {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingFromAscendingOrder = Checkbox::Toggle(_This, _Control as CMlFrame);
			UserStore::SetTrackBrowser_SortOption2(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingFromAscendingOrder);
		}
	}
}

Void SelectOfficialCampaign(CMlScript _This, Integer _ScrollKey) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns.existskey(_ScrollKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[_ScrollKey].existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey)) {
		declare HasPermission = False;
		declare PermissionMessage = "";
		declare LiveQuarterlyCampaign = CampaignStore::GetLiveQuarterlyCampaign();
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[_ScrollKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey].Id == LiveQuarterlyCampaign.Id) {
			HasPermission = UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_PlayCurrentOfficialQuarterlyCampaign);
			if (!HasPermission) PermissionMessage = RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_PlayCurrentOfficialQuarterlyCampaign);
		} else {
			HasPermission = UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_PlayPastOfficialQuarterlyCampaign);
			if (!HasPermission) PermissionMessage = RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_PlayPastOfficialQuarterlyCampaign);
		}

		if (!HasPermission) {
			ClubEdition::GoToPage(_This, Router::GetCurrentRoutePath(_This), PermissionMessage);
		} else {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey = _ScrollKey;
			UnfocusLastOfficialCampaign(_This);
			GoToSection(_This, C_Section_SelectedOfficialCampaign);
		}
	}
}

Void SelectMonthly(CMlScript _This, Integer _ScrollKey) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey = _ScrollKey;
	UnfocusLastMonthly(_This, False);
	GoToSection(_This, C_Section_SelectedMonthly);
}

Void SelectRoyal(CMlScript _This, Integer _ScrollKey) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals.existskey(_ScrollKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals[_ScrollKey].existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey)) {
		if (!UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_PlayMatchmaking)) { // use same permission than the one used in the LIVE menu to play a Royal match
			ClubEdition::GoToPage(_This, Router::GetCurrentRoutePath(_This), RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_PlayRoyalTracks));
		} else {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey = _ScrollKey;
			UnfocusLastMonthly(_This, True);
			GoToSection(_This, C_Section_SelectedRoyal);
		}
	}
}

Void AddTrackToSelection(CMlScript _This, Integer _TrackKey, CMlFrame _Frame_Track) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare Text TrackUid;
	declare CampaignStruct::LibCampaignStruct_K_Map CurrentTrack;
	declare Boolean IsSelected;
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks) {
		CurrentTrack = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[_TrackKey].TrackInfo;
	} else {
		CurrentTrack = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks[_TrackKey];
	}
	TrackUid = CurrentTrack.Uid;
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks.existskey(TrackUid)) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks.removekey(TrackUid);
		IsSelected = False;
	}	else {
		if (
			!UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_PlayEntireOfficialQuarterlyCampaign) &&
			RBAC::TrackRequiresEntireCampaignAccess(CampaignStore::GetLiveQuarterlyCampaign(), TrackUid)
		) {
			IsSelected = False;
			ClubEdition::GoToPage(_This, Router::GetCurrentRoutePath(_This), RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_PlayEntireOfficialQuarterlyCampaign));
		} else {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks[TrackUid] = CurrentTrack;
			IsSelected = True;
		}
	}
	UpdateSelectedTrack(_This, _Frame_Track, IsSelected);
	CheckButtonSelectAllTracks(_This);
}

Void SelectTrack(CMlScript _This, Integer _TrackKey, CMlFrame _Frame_Track, CampaignStruct::LibCampaignStruct_K_Map _TrackInfo) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare HasPermission = False;
	declare PermissionMessage = "";
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.IsBrowsingForEdition) {
		if (_TrackInfo.CreatedWithSimpleEditor) {
			HasPermission = UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_OpenSimpleMapEditor);
			if (!HasPermission) PermissionMessage = RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_OpenSimpleMapEditor);
		} else {
			HasPermission = UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_OpenAdvancedMapEditor);
			if (!HasPermission) PermissionMessage = RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_OpenAdvancedMapEditor);
		}
	}

	declare K_CheckPermissionTOTD CheckPermissionTOTD;
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedMonthly) {
		CheckPermissionTOTD = CheckPermissionTOTD(
			_This,
			<Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey>,
			_TrackInfo.Uid
		);
	}

	if (
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedMonthly &&
		!CheckPermissionTOTD.HasPermission
	) {
		ClubEdition::GoToPage(_This, Router::GetCurrentRoutePath(_This), CheckPermissionTOTD.PermissionMessage);
	} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.IsBrowsingForEdition && !HasPermission) {
		ClubEdition::GoToPage(_This, Router::GetCurrentRoutePath(_This), PermissionMessage);
	} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect) {
		AddTrackToSelection(_This, _TrackKey, _Frame_Track);
	} else {
		if (
			!UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_PlayEntireOfficialQuarterlyCampaign) &&
			RBAC::TrackRequiresEntireCampaignAccess(CampaignStore::GetLiveQuarterlyCampaign(), _TrackInfo.Uid)
		) {
			ClubEdition::GoToPage(_This, Router::GetCurrentRoutePath(_This), RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_PlayEntireOfficialQuarterlyCampaign);
		} else {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.PendingEvents.add(K_Event{
				Type = C_Event_Select,
				Track = _TrackInfo
			});
		}
	}
}

Void OpenPopUp_DeleteLocalTrack(CMlScript _This, Integer _TrackKey) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.existskey(_TrackKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[_TrackKey].SubFolder == "") {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Name = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[_TrackKey].TrackInfo.Name;
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.FileName = TL::Replace(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[_TrackKey].TrackInfo.LocalFileName, "\\", "/");
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Uid = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[_TrackKey].TrackInfo.Uid;
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus = Task::DestroyAndCreate(
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus,
			DataFileMgr,
			DataFileMgr.Map_NadeoServices_GetFromUid(MainUser::GetMainUserId(), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Uid)
		);

		PopUpMultiChoice::SetTitle(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, C_DeleteTrackPopUp_Title, False);
		PopUpMultiChoice::SetDescription(_This,
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice,
			[
				PopUpMultiChoice::CreateDescriptionPart(TL::Compose(C_DeleteTrackPopUp_Description1, "$<"^Tools::FormatValue(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Name)^"$>"), <130., 15.>, 3., Stylesheet::GetFont(Stylesheet::C_Font_Weight_Regular), "$t$i", <1., 1., 1.>, False)
			],
			False
		);
		PopUpMultiChoice::SetClosedAfterSelection(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, True);
		PopUpMultiChoice::SetStylesSecondChoice(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, [ExpendableButton_Trackmania::C_Style_SizeExpendable, ExpendableButton_Trackmania::C_Style_AlignCenter, ExpendableButton_Trackmania::C_Style_ButtonSecondary, ExpendableButton_Trackmania::C_Style_ButtonWarning], False);
		PopUpMultiChoice::SetChoices(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, C_DeleteTrackPopUp_Choices, False);
		PopUpMultiChoice::RedrawPopUpMultiChoice(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, False);
		declare Integer PopUpType for Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice;
		PopUpType = C_PopUpDeleteTrackIndex;
		PopUpMultiChoice::Open(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice);
	}
}

Void SetLoadingSpinnerPopUp(CMlScript _This, Boolean _IsLoading, Text _Label, Boolean _ForceRedraw) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	if (_IsLoading)	{
		LoadingSpinner::StartAnimation(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner_PopUp, _Label);
		PopUpMultiChoice::ResetDescription(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, False);
	} else {
		LoadingSpinner::StopAnimation(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner_PopUp);
	}
	PopUpMultiChoice::SetForceHideChoices(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, _IsLoading, _ForceRedraw);
	PopUpMultiChoice::LockPopUp(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, _IsLoading, True);
}

Void SetLoadingSpinnerPopUp(CMlScript _This, Boolean _IsLoading, Text _Label) {
	SetLoadingSpinnerPopUp(_This, _IsLoading, _Label, True);
}

Void EditUploadLocalTrackPopUp(
	CMlScript _This,
	Boolean _TrackIsValid,
	Boolean _WaitingForTrackData,
	Boolean _TrackAlreadyUploaded,
	Boolean _TrackUploadedByMe,
	Boolean _NewUploadComplete,
	Text _NewUploadError
) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	declare Text Title = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Title1;
	declare Text[Integer] Choices = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Choices;
	declare Text Description1 = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description1;
	declare Text Description2 = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description2;
	declare Vec3 ColorDescription2 = <1., 1., 1.>;
	declare PopUpMultiChoice::K_DescriptionPart[] Description;

	if (_NewUploadComplete) {
		if (_NewUploadError != "") {
			Title = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Title4;
			Description1 = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description11;
			Description2 = TL::Compose( C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description12, _NewUploadError);
			ColorDescription2 = Stylesheet::GetColorRGB(Stylesheet::C_Color_TextError);
			Choices.removekey(C_UploadTrackPopUp_ChoiceIndex_Upload);
		} else {
			Title = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Title3;
			Description1 = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description9;
			Description2 = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description10;
			ColorDescription2 = Stylesheet::GetColorRGB(Stylesheet::C_Color_AccentOne);
			Choices.removekey(C_UploadTrackPopUp_ChoiceIndex_Upload);
		}
	} else {
		if (_TrackIsValid && !_WaitingForTrackData) {
			if (_TrackAlreadyUploaded) {
				Title = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Title2;
				if (_TrackUploadedByMe) {
					Description1 = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description3;
					Description2 = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description4;
					ColorDescription2 = Stylesheet::GetColorRGB(Stylesheet::C_Color_AccentOne);
				} else {
					Description1 = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description7;
					Description2 = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description8;
					Choices.removekey(C_UploadTrackPopUp_ChoiceIndex_Upload);
				}
			}
		} else {
			Description1 = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description5;
			Description2 = C_UploadTrackPopUp_Description6;
			ColorDescription2 = Stylesheet::GetColorRGB(Stylesheet::C_Color_AccentOne);
			Choices.removekey(C_UploadTrackPopUp_ChoiceIndex_Upload);
		}
	}

	Description = [
		PopUpMultiChoice::CreateDescriptionPart(TL::Compose(Description1, "$<"^Tools::FormatValue(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Name)^"$>"), <130., 15.>, 3., Stylesheet::GetFont(Stylesheet::C_Font_Weight_Regular), "$t$i", <1., 1., 1.>, False),
		PopUpMultiChoice::CreateDescriptionPart(Description2, <130., 10.>, 3., Stylesheet::GetFont(Stylesheet::C_Font_Weight_SemiBold), "$t$i", ColorDescription2, False)
	];

	PopUpMultiChoice::SetTitle(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, Title, False);
	PopUpMultiChoice::SetDescription(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, Description, False);
	PopUpMultiChoice::SetChoices(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, Choices, False);
	SetLoadingSpinnerPopUp(_This, _WaitingForTrackData, C_Text_CheckingTrackOnline, False);
	PopUpMultiChoice::RedrawPopUpMultiChoice(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, False);
}

Void OpenPopUp_UploadLocalTrack(CMlScript _This, Integer _TrackKey) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.existskey(_TrackKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[_TrackKey].SubFolder == "") {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Name = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[_TrackKey].TrackInfo.Name;
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Uid = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[_TrackKey].TrackInfo.Uid;
		PopUpMultiChoice::SetStylesSecondChoice(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, [ExpendableButton_Trackmania::C_Style_SizeExpendable, ExpendableButton_Trackmania::C_Style_AlignCenter, ExpendableButton_Trackmania::C_Style_ButtonSecondary], False);
		PopUpMultiChoice::SetClosedAfterSelection(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, False);

		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[_TrackKey].TrackInfo.IsPlayable) {
			EditUploadLocalTrackPopUp(_This, True, True, False, False, False, "");
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus = Task::DestroyAndCreate(
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus,
				DataFileMgr,
				DataFileMgr.Map_NadeoServices_GetFromUid(MainUser::GetMainUserId(), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Uid)
			);
		} else {
			EditUploadLocalTrackPopUp(_This, False, False, False, False, False, "");
		}
		declare Integer PopUpType for Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice;
		PopUpType = C_PopUpUploadTrackIndex;
		PopUpMultiChoice::Open(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice);
	}
}

Void OpenPopUp_RemoveFavoriteTrack(CMlScript _This, Integer _TrackKey) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks.existskey(_TrackKey)) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.RemoveTrack.Name = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks[_TrackKey].Name;

		PopUpMultiChoice::SetTitle(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, C_RemoveFavoriteMapPopUp_Title, False);
		PopUpMultiChoice::SetDescription(_This,
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice,
			[
				PopUpMultiChoice::CreateDescriptionPart(TL::Compose(C_RemoveFavoriteMapPopUp_Description1, "$<"^Tools::FormatValue(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.RemoveTrack.Name)^"$>"), <130., 15.>, 3., Stylesheet::GetFont(Stylesheet::C_Font_Weight_Regular), "$t$i", <1., 1., 1.>, False),
				PopUpMultiChoice::CreateDescriptionPart(C_RemoveFavoriteMapPopUp_Description2, <130., 10.>, 3., Stylesheet::GetFont(Stylesheet::C_Font_Weight_SemiBold), "$t$i", Stylesheet::GetColorRGB(Stylesheet::C_Color_AccentOne), False)
			],
			False
		);
		PopUpMultiChoice::SetClosedAfterSelection(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, True);
		PopUpMultiChoice::SetStylesSecondChoice(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, [ExpendableButton_Trackmania::C_Style_SizeExpendable, ExpendableButton_Trackmania::C_Style_AlignCenter, ExpendableButton_Trackmania::C_Style_ButtonSecondary, ExpendableButton_Trackmania::C_Style_ButtonWarning], False);
		PopUpMultiChoice::SetChoices(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, C_RemoveFavoriteMapPopUp_Choices, False);
		PopUpMultiChoice::RedrawPopUpMultiChoice(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice, False);
		declare Integer PopUpType for Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice;
		PopUpType = C_PopUpRemoveFavoriteTrackIndex;
		PopUpMultiChoice::Open(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice);
	}
}

Void AddOrRemoveFocusedTrackToFavorites(CMlScript _This, Integer _TrackKey) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks.existskey(_TrackKey) && Now > Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.LastAddOrRemoveRequestTime + C_FavoriteTrackRequestCooldown) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CurrentTrackUid = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks[_TrackKey].Uid;
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CurrentTrackName = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks[_TrackKey].Name;
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.LastAddOrRemoveRequestTime = Now;
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.KnownedFavoritesTracksUids.exists(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CurrentTrackUid)) {
			MapStore::Action_RemoveMapFromFavorites(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CurrentTrackUid);
		} else {
			MapStore::Action_AddMapToFavorites(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CurrentTrackUid);
		}
	}
}

Void ShowError(CMlScript _This, Text _ErrorMessage) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_Error.Value = _ErrorMessage;
	Tools::FitLabelValue(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_Error, 4., 2., 0.25);
}

Boolean Private_IsScrollTracksDisplayed(Integer _TabIndex, Integer _Section) {
	return (
		_TabIndex == C_TabIndex_Favorites ||
		_Section == C_Section_LocalTracks ||
		_Section == C_Section_OnlineTracks ||
		_Section == C_Section_SelectedOfficialCampaign ||
		_Section == C_Section_SelectedMonthly ||
		_Section == C_Section_SelectedRoyal ||
		_Section == C_Section_SelectedClubCampaign
	);
}

Void Private_ProcessStoreEvents(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;

	foreach (Event in _This.PendingEvents) {
		switch (Event.Type) {
			case CMlScriptEvent::Type::PluginCustomEvent: {
				switch (Event.CustomEventType) {
					case UserStore::C_Event_MatchmakingInfosUpdated: {
						UpdateRoyalVictoriesDisplay(_This);
					}
