					case MapStore::C_Event_FavoriteMapsUpdated, MapStore::C_Event_FavoriteMapsError: {
						if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Favorites) {
							Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks = MapStore::GetFavoriteMaps();
							Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, MapStore::GetFavoriteMapsTotal());
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.IsLoadingTracks) {
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.IsLoadingTracks = False;
								UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
							}
							if (Event.CustomEventType == MapStore::C_Event_FavoriteMapsError) {
								if (Event.CustomEventData.count > 1)  {
									ShowError(_This, Event.CustomEventData[1]);
								}
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
							}
						}
					}
					case MapStore::C_Event_CurrentMapUpdated: {
						// Retrieve map name and uid depending on the current tab
						declare Text TrackUid = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CurrentTrackUid;
						declare Text TrackName = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CurrentTrackName;
						if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Favorites) {
							TrackUid = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.RemoveTrack.Uid;
							TrackName = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.RemoveTrack.Name;
						}

						declare MapStore::K_CurrentMap CurrentMap = MapStore::GetCurrentMap();

						// Display error if necessary
						if (CurrentMap.Status == MapStore::C_CurrentMapStatus_Error) {
							if (CurrentMap.ErrorCode == MapStore::C_ErrorCode_FailedRemoveFavorites) {
								ShowError(_This, Error::GetErrorMessage(Error::C_Type_ManiaScript, Error::C_Code_TrackBrowser_RemoveFavoriteMap, "HTTP "^CurrentMap.ErrorCodeHttp, ["$<"^Tools::FormatValue(TrackName)^"$>"]));
							} else if (CurrentMap.ErrorCode == MapStore::C_ErrorCode_FailedAddFavorites) {
								ShowError(_This, Error::GetErrorMessage(Error::C_Type_ManiaScript, Error::C_Code_TrackBrowser_AddFavoriteMap, "HTTP "^CurrentMap.ErrorCodeHttp, ["$<"^Tools::FormatValue(TrackName)^"$>"]));
							}
							Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
						} else if (CurrentMap.Status == MapStore::C_CurrentMapStatus_Success && TrackUid == CurrentMap.Uid) {
							Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_Error.Value = "";
							// In the rare case where we have the same map several times in a campaign, we check all tracks
							foreach (I => Track in Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks) {
								if (Track.Uid == TrackUid) {
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks[I].IsFavorite = CurrentMap.IsFavorite;
								}
							}
							if (CurrentMap.IsFavorite) Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.KnownedFavoritesTracksUids.add(TrackUid);
							else Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.KnownedFavoritesTracksUids.remove(TrackUid);

							// Remove track from selected tracks if necessary
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Favorites) {
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect) Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks.removekey(TrackUid);
							} else { // Update favorite heart icon
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks);
							}
						}

						// Reset map uid and name at the end
						if (CurrentMap.Status == MapStore::C_CurrentMapStatus_Success || CurrentMap.Status == MapStore::C_CurrentMapStatus_Error) {
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Favorites) {
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.RemoveTrack.Name = "";
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.RemoveTrack.Uid = "";
								Refresh(_This);
							} else {
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CurrentTrackUid = "";
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CurrentTrackName = "";
							}
						}
					}
					case CampaignStore::C_Event_LiveQuarterlyCampaignUpdated: {
						if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Official && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_OfficialCampaigns) {
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingCampaigns) {
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingCampaigns = False;
								UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
							}
							declare Status = CampaignStore::GetLiveQuarterlyCampaignStatus();
							if (Status == CampaignStore::C_LiveCampaignStatus_Loaded) {
								SortOfficialCampaigns(_This, CampaignStore::GetLiveQuarterlyCampaign());
								Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Official_Campaigns, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns.count);
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey != -1 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentCampaign) {
									Scroll::ScrollToElement(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Official_Campaigns, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey, True);
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentCampaign = False;
								}
							} else if (Status == CampaignStore::C_LiveCampaignStatus_NoCampaigns || Status == CampaignStore::C_LiveCampaignStatus_Error) {
								Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Official_Campaigns, 0);
								if (Status == CampaignStore::C_LiveCampaignStatus_Error) {
									//L16N Error while retrieving the official campaigns
									ShowError(_This, TL::Compose(_("Error while retrieving the official campaigns. (Error code: %1)"), Error::C_Code_TrackBrowser_GetOfficialCampaigns));
									Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
								}
							}
						}
					}
					case CampaignStore::C_Event_CampaignListUpdated,
							CampaignStore::C_Event_MonthlyCampaignLoadComplete,
							CampaignStore::C_Event_RoyalCampaignLoadComplete,
							CampaignStore::C_Event_CampaignListEmpty,
							CampaignStore::C_Event_CampaignListUpdateError: {
						if (
							(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Official &&
								(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedOfficialCampaign ||
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Monthly ||
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedMonthly ||
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal ||
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedRoyal
								)
							) ||
							(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Clubs && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedClubCampaign)
						) {
							declare Boolean IsValidCampaign = False;
							// Monthly campaign selected
							if (Event.CustomEventType == CampaignStore::C_Event_MonthlyCampaignLoadComplete && Event.CustomEventData.count > 0 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedMonthly) {
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey].existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey)) {
									declare K_MonthlyCampaign CurrentCampaign = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey];
									if (TL::ToInteger(Event.CustomEventData[0]) == CurrentCampaign.Id) {
										IsValidCampaign = True;
										UpdateOfficialTracks(_This);
									} else {
										Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, 0);
										Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingTracks = False;
										UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
									}
								}
							} else if (Event.CustomEventType == CampaignStore::C_Event_RoyalCampaignLoadComplete && Event.CustomEventData.count > 0 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedRoyal) {
								// Royal campaign selected
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey].existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey)) {
									declare K_MonthlyCampaign CurrentCampaign = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey];
									if (TL::ToInteger(Event.CustomEventData[0]) == CurrentCampaign.Id) {
										IsValidCampaign = True;
										UpdateOfficialTracks(_This);
									} else {
										Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, 0);
										Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingTracks = False;
										UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
									}
								}
							} else if (Event.CustomEventData.count > 0) {
								declare Integer CampaignType = TL::ToInteger(Event.CustomEventData[0]);
								// Official campaign selected
								if (CampaignType == CampaignStruct::C_CampaignType_Quarterly && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedOfficialCampaign) {
									declare CampaignList = CampaignStore::GetCampaignList(CampaignStruct::C_CampaignType_Quarterly);
									if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey].existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey)) {
										declare Integer Key = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey].OffsetKey;
										if (CampaignList.existskey(Key) && CampaignList[Key].Id != CampaignStruct::C_Campaign_NullId) {
											IsValidCampaign = True;
											Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey].Id = CampaignList[Key].Id;
											UpdateOfficialTracks(_This);
										} else {
											Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, 0);
											Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingTracks = False;
											UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
										}
									}
								} else if (CampaignType == CampaignStruct::C_CampaignType_Monthly) {
									// List of monthly campaigns
									if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Monthly) {
										if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingMonthly) {
											Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingMonthly = False;
											UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
										}
										SortMonthlies(_This, CampaignStore::GetMonthlyCampaignList(), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.ScrollMonthlyOffset, False);
										Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies.count);
										if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey != -1 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentMonthly) {
											Scroll::ScrollToElement(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey, True);
											Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentMonthly = False;
										}
									} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedMonthly) { // Monthly campaign selected with no campaign id
										declare CampaignList = CampaignStore::GetMonthlyCampaignList();
										if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey].existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey)) {
											declare Integer Key = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey].OffsetKey;
											if (CampaignList.existskey(Key) && CampaignList[Key].Id != CampaignStruct::C_Campaign_NullId) {
												IsValidCampaign = True;
												Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.MonthlyColumnFocusKey].Id = CampaignList[Key].Id;
												UpdateOfficialTracks(_This);
											} else {
												Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, 0);
												Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingTracks = False;
												UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
											}
										}
									}
								} else if (CampaignType == CampaignStruct::C_CampaignType_Royal) {
									// List of royal campaigns
									if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal) {
										if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingRoyal) {
											Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingRoyal = False;
											UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
										}
										SortMonthlies(_This, CampaignStore::GetRoyalCampaignList(), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.ScrollRoyalOffset, True);
										Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals.count);
										if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey != -1 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentRoyal) {
											Scroll::ScrollToElement(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey, True);
											Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.FocusParentRoyal = False;
										}
									} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedRoyal) { // Royal campaign selected with no campaign id
										declare CampaignList = CampaignStore::GetRoyalCampaignList();
										if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey].existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey)) {
											declare Integer Key = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey].OffsetKey;
											if (CampaignList.existskey(Key) && CampaignList[Key].Id != CampaignStruct::C_Campaign_NullId) {
												IsValidCampaign = True;
												Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.RoyalColumnFocusKey].Id = CampaignList[Key].Id;
												UpdateOfficialTracks(_This);
											} else {
												Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, 0);
												Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingTracks = False;
												UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
							// Stop loading if error on selected campaign
							if (Event.CustomEventType == CampaignStore::C_Event_CampaignListUpdateError && (Event.CustomEventData.count < 3 || Event.CustomEventData[2] != CampaignStore::C_ErrorType_ScoresNotLoaded)) {
								Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, 0);
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.IsLoadingTracks = False;
								UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedMonthly) {
									//L16N Error while retrieving the tracks of the selected month
									ShowError(_This, TL::Compose(_("Error while retrieving this month tracks. (Error code: %1)"), Error::C_Code_TrackBrowser_GetMonthlyTracks));
								} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedOfficialCampaign) {
									//L16N Error while retrieving an official campaign
									ShowError(_This, TL::Compose(_("Error while retrieving this official campaign. (Error code: %1)"), Error::C_Code_TrackBrowser_GetOfficialCampaignTracks));
								} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedClubCampaign) {
									//L16N Error while retrieving a club campaign
									ShowError(_This, TL::Compose(_("Error while retrieving this club campaign. (Error code: %1)"), Error::C_Code_TrackBrowser_GetClubCampaignTracks));
								}
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
							}
						}
					}
					case ClubStore::C_Event_BrowserClubsUpdated, ClubStore::C_Event_BrowserClubsError: {
						if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Clubs && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_None) {
							Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.Clubs = ClubStore::GetBrowserClubs();
							Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs, ClubStore::GetBrowserClubsTotal());
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.IsLoadingClubs) {
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.IsLoadingClubs = False;
								UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
							}
							if (Event.CustomEventType == ClubStore::C_Event_BrowserClubsError) {
								//L16N Error while retrieving player's clubs
								ShowError(_This, TL::Compose(_("Error while retrieving your clubs. (Error code: %1)"), Error::C_Code_TrackBrowser_GetPlayerClubs));
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
							}
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClubKey != -1 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.FocusParentClub) {
								Scroll::ScrollToElement(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClubKey, True);
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClubKey = -1;
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.FocusParentClub = False;
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClub = ClubStruct::LibStructuresClub_K_Club {};
							}
						}
					}
					case CampaignStore::C_Event_ClubsCampaignListUpdated, CampaignStore::C_Event_ClubsCampaignListError: {
						if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Clubs && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedClub) {
							Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns = CampaignStore::GetClubCampaignList(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClub.Id);
							Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs, CampaignStore::GetClubCampaignsTotal(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClub.Id));
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.IsLoadingCampaigns) {
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.IsLoadingCampaigns = False;
								UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
							}
							if (Event.CustomEventType == CampaignStore::C_Event_ClubsCampaignListError) {
								//L16N Error while retrieving the current club campaigns, %1 will be replaced by the club name, %2 by a code, e.g "Error while retrieving 'Darrek' club campaigns. (Error code: 400)"
								ShowError(_This, TL::Compose(_("Error while retrieving '%1' club campaigns. (Error code: %2)"), TL::StripFormatting(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClub.Name), Error::C_Code_TrackBrowser_GetClubCampaigns));
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
							}
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaignKey != -1 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.FocusParentCampaign) {
								Scroll::ScrollToElement(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaignKey, True);
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaignKey = -1;
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.FocusParentCampaign = False;
							}
						}
					}
					case CampaignStore::C_Event_CampaignLoadComplete: {
						if (
							(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Official && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedOfficialCampaign) ||
							(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Clubs && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedClubCampaign)
						) {
							declare Integer SelectedClubCampaignId = CampaignStruct::C_Campaign_NullId;
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaignKey)) {
								SelectedClubCampaignId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaignKey].Id;
							}
							declare Integer OfficialCampaignId = CampaignStruct::C_Campaign_NullId;
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns.existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey) && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey].existskey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey)) {
								OfficialCampaignId = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignLineSelectedKey][Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CampaignColumnFocusKey].Id;
							}
							if (Event.CustomEventData.count > 0) {
								declare Integer EventCampaignId = TL::ToInteger(Event.CustomEventData[0]);
								if (SelectedClubCampaignId == EventCampaignId) {
									UpdateClubCampaignTracks(_This, SelectedClubCampaignId);
								} else if (OfficialCampaignId == EventCampaignId) {
									UpdateOfficialTracks(_This);
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

Void Private_ProcessScrollEvents(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;

	foreach (Event in Scroll::GetPendingEvents(_This)) {
		if (Event.Scroll != Null) {
			switch (Event.Scroll.Id) {
				case Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks.Id: {
					switch (Event.Type) {
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Cancel: if (!LoadingSpinner::IsLoading(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner)) Cancel(_This);
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Select: {
							// Special behavior for Local Tracks due to sub folders
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks) {
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.existskey(Event.ToKey)) {
									if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[Event.ToKey].SubFolder != "") {
										UpdateLocalTracks(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[Event.ToKey].SubFolder);
										Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LastFolderSelected_Keys.add(Event.ToKey);
									} else {
										if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.existskey(Event.ToKey)) {
											SelectTrack(_This, Event.ToKey, Event.To, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[Event.ToKey].TrackInfo);
										}
									}
								}
							} else {
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks.existskey(Event.ToKey)) {
									SelectTrack(_This, Event.ToKey, Event.To, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks[Event.ToKey]);
								}
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_PagerUpdate: {
							switch (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection) {
								case C_Section_None: {
									if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Favorites) UpdateFavoriteTracks(_This, Event.PagerOffset, Event.PagerCount);
								}
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Update: {
							// Special behavior for Local Tracks due to sub folders
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks) {
								foreach (Key => Frame_Element in Event.ElementsVisible) {
									declare Integer TrackScrollKey for Frame_Element;
									TrackScrollKey = Key;
									if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.existskey(Key)) {
										if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[Key].SubFolder != "") {
											ShowTrack(_This, Frame_Element, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[Key].TrackInfo, True, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[Key].SubFolder, "");
										} else {
											ShowTrack(_This, Frame_Element, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks[Key].TrackInfo);
										}
									}
								}
								foreach (Key => Frame_Element in Event.ElementsHidden) {
									declare Integer TrackScrollKey for Frame_Element;
									TrackScrollKey = -1;
									HideTrack(Frame_Element);
								}
							} else {
								foreach (Key => Frame_Element in Event.ElementsVisible) {
									declare Integer TrackScrollKey for Frame_Element;
									TrackScrollKey = Key;
									if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks.existskey(Key)) {
										if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedMonthly || Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedRoyal) {
											declare Text MonthDay = TL::FormatInteger(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentMonthDays[Key], 2);
											ShowTrack(_This, Frame_Element, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks[Key], MonthDay);
										} else {
											ShowTrack(_This, Frame_Element, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks[Key]);
										}
									} else {
										ShowTrackLoading(_This, Frame_Element);
									}
								}
								foreach (Key => Frame_Element in Event.ElementsHidden) {
									declare Integer TrackScrollKey for Frame_Element;
									TrackScrollKey = -1;
									HideTrack(Frame_Element);
								}
							}
							Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks.Visible = Event.ElementsVisible.count > 0;
							LockScroll(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, Event.ElementsVisible.count <= 0);
							UpdateNoTracksMessage(_This, Event.ElementsVisible.count);
							if (Event.ElementsVisible.count > 0 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.Visible) {
								CheckButtonSelectAllTracks(_This);
							}
							if (Private_IsScrollTracksDisplayed(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection)) {
								if (Event.ElementsVisible.count > 0) {
									Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks);
								} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_NoTracks.Visible) {
									Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
								}
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Focus: {
							if (Event.From != Null) FocusTrack(_This, Event.From, False);
							if (Event.To != Null) {
								if (Event.IsMouse && !Scroll::IsFocused(Event.Scroll)) {
									Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Event.Scroll);
								}
								if (Scroll::IsFocused(Event.Scroll)) {
									FocusTrack(_This, Event.To, True);
								}
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_ReachLimit: {
							if (Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Down) {
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_AddTracks.Visible) Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_AddTracks);
								else Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
							} else if (Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Left) {
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
							} else if (Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Up && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Options.Visible) {
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.LastOptionButtonFocused.Visible) {
									Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.LastOptionButtonFocused);
								} else {
									foreach (Control in Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Options.Controls) {
										if (Navigation::IsNavigationControl(Control) && !Navigation::IsLocked(Control)) {
											Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Control);
										}
									}
								}
							} else if (Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Right && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_AddTracks.Visible) {
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_AddTracks);
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_NavAction: {
							if (Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Action1) {
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks && !Task::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task)) {
									OpenPopUp_DeleteLocalTrack(_This, Event.ToKey);
								} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Favorites) {
									OpenPopUp_RemoveFavoriteTrack(_This, Event.ToKey);
								}
							} else if (Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Action2) {
								if (
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks &&
									!Task::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus) &&
									!Task::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task)
								) {
									OpenPopUp_UploadLocalTrack(_This, Event.ToKey);
								} else if (
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection != C_Section_None &&
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection != C_Section_LocalTracks
								) {
									AddOrRemoveFocusedTrackToFavorites(_This, Event.ToKey);
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				case Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Official_Campaigns.Id: {
					switch (Event.Type) {
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Cancel: if (!LoadingSpinner::IsLoading(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner)) Cancel(_This);
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Select: SelectOfficialCampaign(_This, Event.ToKey);
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Update: {
							foreach (Key => Frame_Element in Event.ElementsVisible) {
								declare Integer CampaignScrollKey for Frame_Element;
								CampaignScrollKey = Key;
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns.existskey(Key)) {
									declare CMlControl[] CampaignFrames = GetLineControls(Frame_Element);
									foreach (I => Element in CampaignFrames) {
										if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[Key].existskey(I)) {
											ShowClubOrCampaign((Element as CMlFrame), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[Key][I].Name, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[Key][I].ImageUrl, ""^Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Campaigns[Key][I].Year, (I == 0));
										} else {
											HideClubOrCampaign(Element as CMlFrame);
										}
									}
								}
							}
							foreach (Key => Frame_Element in Event.ElementsHidden) {
								declare Integer CampaignScrollKey for Frame_Element;
								CampaignScrollKey = Key;
								declare CMlControl[] CampaignFrames = GetLineControls(Frame_Element);
								foreach (I => Element in CampaignFrames) {
									HideClubOrCampaign(Element as CMlFrame, True, (I == 0));
								}
							}
							Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Official_Campaigns.Visible = Event.ElementsVisible.count > 0;
							LockScroll(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Official_Campaigns, Event.ElementsVisible.count <= 0);
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_OfficialCampaigns) UpdateNoTracksMessage(_This, Event.ElementsVisible.count);
							if (Event.ElementsVisible.count > 0) {
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Official_Campaigns);
							} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_NoTracks.Visible) {
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Focus: {
							if (Event.From != Null) {
								FocusOfficialCampaign(_This, Event.From, False);
							}
							if (Event.To != Null) {
								if (Event.IsMouse && !Scroll::IsFocused(Event.Scroll)) {
									Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Event.Scroll);
								}
								if (Scroll::IsFocused(Event.Scroll)) {
									FocusOfficialCampaign(_This, Event.To, True);
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollCampaignFocus = Event.To;
								}
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_ReachLimit: {
							if ((Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Right || Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Left) && Event.From != Null) {
								FocusOfficialCampaignByInput(_This, Event.NavAction, Event.From);
							} else if (Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Down) {
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
							}
						}
					}
				}
				case Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD.Id: {
					switch (Event.Type) {
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Cancel: if (!LoadingSpinner::IsLoading(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner)) Cancel(_This);
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Select: {
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Monthly) SelectMonthly(_This, Event.ToKey);
							else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal) SelectRoyal(_This, Event.ToKey);
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Update: {
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Monthly && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageMonthly != Event.Page) {
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageMonthly = Event.Page;
								declare Integer Length = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.ManialinkProps.MonthlyPerPage * 3;
								declare Integer Offset = ML::Max(0, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageMonthly - 2) * Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.ManialinkProps.MonthlyPerPage;
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.ScrollMonthlyOffset = ML::Max(0, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageMonthly - 2) * Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.ManialinkProps.TOTDPerPage;
								CampaignStore::Action_LoadMonthlyCampaignsList(_This, Offset, Length);
							} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageRoyal != Event.Page) {
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageRoyal = Event.Page;
								declare Integer Length = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.ManialinkProps.MonthlyPerPage * 3;
								declare Integer Offset = ML::Max(0, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageRoyal - 2) * Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.ManialinkProps.MonthlyPerPage;
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.ScrollRoyalOffset = ML::Max(0, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.CurrentPageRoyal - 2) * Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.ManialinkProps.TOTDPerPage;
								CampaignStore::Action_LoadRoyalCampaignsList(_This, Offset, Length);
							}

							foreach (Key => Frame_Element in Event.ElementsVisible) {
								declare Integer MonthlyScrollKey for Frame_Element;
								MonthlyScrollKey = Key;
								declare CMlControl[] TOTD_Frames = GetLineControls(Frame_Element);
								declare K_MonthlyCampaign[][Integer] CurrentMonthlies = [];
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Monthly) {
									CurrentMonthlies = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Monthlies;
								} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal) {
									CurrentMonthlies = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.Royals;
								}
								if (CurrentMonthlies.existskey(Key)) {
									foreach (I => Element in TOTD_Frames) {
										if (CurrentMonthlies[Key].existskey(I)) {
											declare Text MonthNumber = TL::FormatInteger(CurrentMonthlies[Key][I].MonthNumber, 2);
											ShowTOTD((Element as CMlFrame), CurrentMonthlies[Key][I].MonthName, MonthNumber, ""^CurrentMonthlies[Key][I].Year, CurrentMonthlies[Key][I].YearFormat, (I == 0));
										} else {
											HideTOTD(Element as CMlFrame, False, False);
										}
									}
								}
							}
							foreach (Key => Frame_Element in Event.ElementsHidden) {
								declare Integer MonthlyScrollKey for Frame_Element;
								MonthlyScrollKey = Key;
								declare CMlControl[] TOTD_Frames = GetLineControls(Frame_Element);
								foreach (I => Element in TOTD_Frames) {
									HideTOTD(Element as CMlFrame, True, (I == 0));
								}
							}
							Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD.Visible = Event.ElementsVisible.count > 0;
							LockScroll(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD, Event.ElementsVisible.count <= 0);
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Monthly || Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal) {
								UpdateNoTracksMessage(_This, Event.ElementsVisible.count);
								if (Event.ElementsVisible.count > 0) {
									Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD);
								} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_NoTracks.Visible) {
									Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
								}
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Focus: {
							if (Event.From != Null) {
								FocusMonthly(_This, Event.From, False, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal);
							}
							if (Event.To != Null) {
								if (Event.IsMouse && !Scroll::IsFocused(Event.Scroll)) {
									Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Event.Scroll);
								}
								if (Scroll::IsFocused(Event.Scroll)) {
									FocusMonthly(_This, Event.To, True, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal);
									if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Monthly) Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollMonthlyFocus = Event.To;
									else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal) Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastScrollRoyalFocus = Event.To;
								}
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_ReachLimit: {
							if ((Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Right || Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Left) && Event.From != Null) {
								FocusMonthlyByInput(_This, Event.NavAction, Event.From, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal);
							} else if (Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Down) {
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
							}
						}
					}
				}
				case Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs.Id: {
					switch (Event.Type) {
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Cancel: if (!LoadingSpinner::IsLoading(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner)) Cancel(_This);
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Select: {
							switch (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection) {
								case C_Section_None: {
									if (!UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_ViewClub)) {
										ClubEdition::GoToPage(_This, Router::GetCurrentRoutePath(_This), RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_ViewClub));
									} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.Clubs.existskey(Event.ToKey)) {
										Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClub = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.Clubs[Event.ToKey];
										Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClubKey = Event.ToKey;
										GoToSection(_This, C_Section_SelectedClub);
									}
								}
								case C_Section_SelectedClub: {
									if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns.existskey(Event.ToKey)) {
										if (!UserStore::HasGamePermission(PrivilegeMgr, RBAC::C_GamePermission_JoinClub)) {
											declare PermissionMessage = "";
											if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.IsBrowsingForEdition) {
												PermissionMessage = RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_EditClubMap);
											} else {
												PermissionMessage = RBAC::GetGamePermissionMessage(RBAC::C_GamePermissionMessage_PlayPublicClubCampaign);
											}
											ClubEdition::GoToPage(_This, Router::GetCurrentRoutePath(_This), PermissionMessage);
										} else {
											Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaignKey = Event.ToKey;
											GoToSection(_This, C_Section_SelectedClubCampaign);
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_PagerUpdate: {
							switch (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection) {
								case C_Section_None: {
									ClubStore::Action_LoadClubsBrowser(_This, Event.PagerOffset, Event.PagerCount);
								}
								case C_Section_SelectedClub: {
									CampaignStore::Action_LoadClubsCampaigns(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedClub.Id, Event.PagerOffset, Event.PagerCount);
								}
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Update: {
							foreach (Key => Frame_Element in Event.ElementsVisible) {
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_None && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.Clubs.existskey(Key)) {
									ShowClubOrCampaign(Frame_Element, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.Clubs[Key].Name, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.Clubs[Key].IconUrl);
								} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedClub && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns.existskey(Key)) {
									ShowClubOrCampaign(Frame_Element, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns[Key].Name, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Clubs.SelectedCampaigns[Key].Media.ButtonBackgroundUrl);
								} else {
									ShowClubOrCampaignLoading(Frame_Element);
								}
							}
							foreach (Key => Frame_Element in Event.ElementsHidden) {
								HideClubOrCampaign(Frame_Element);
							}

							Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs.Visible = Event.ElementsVisible.count > 0;
							LockScroll(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs, Event.ElementsVisible.count <= 0);
							if (
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Clubs &&
								(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_None || Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_SelectedClub)
							) {
								UpdateNoTracksMessage(_This, Event.ElementsVisible.count);
							}
							if (Event.ElementsVisible.count > 0) {
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs);
							} else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_NoTracks.Visible) {
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_Focus: {
							if (Event.From != Null) FocusClubOrCampaign(_This, Event.From, False);
							if (Event.To != Null) {
								if (Event.IsMouse && !Scroll::IsFocused(Event.Scroll)) {
									Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Event.Scroll);
								}
								if (Scroll::IsFocused(Event.Scroll)) {
									FocusClubOrCampaign(_This, Event.To, True);
								}
							}
						}
						case Scroll::C_EventType_ReachLimit: {
							if (Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Left || Event.NavAction == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Down) {
								Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

K_Event[] GetPendingEvents(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	return Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.PendingEvents;
}

Void MainInit(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State = C_State_Null;
}

Void MainStart(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State = K_State {
		CurrentTabIndex = C_TabIndex_None,
		CurrentSection = C_Section_None,
		Tracks = [],
		SelectedTracks = [],
		MyTracks = K_MyTracks {
			NeedRefresh = False,
			LocalTracks = [],
			CurrentPath = "",
			CurrentParentPath = "",
			FocusParentFolder = False,
			LastFolderSelected_Keys = [],
			Task_GetLocalTracks = Task::GetEmptyTask(),
			Task_GetOnlineTracks = Task::GetEmptyTask(),
			Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus = Task::GetEmptyTask(),
			DeleteLocalTrack = K_DeleteTrack {
				Task = Task::GetEmptyTask(),
				Name = "",
				FileName = "",
				Uid = ""
			},
			UploadLocalTrack = K_UploadTrack {
				Task = Task::GetEmptyTask(),
				Name = "",
				Uid = ""
			}
		},
		Favorites = K_Favorites {
			IsLoadingTracks = False,
			RemoveTrack = K_RemoveTrack {
				Name = "",
				Uid = ""
			}
		},
		Official = K_Official {
			Campaigns = [],
			IsLoadingCampaigns = False,
			IsLoadingTracks = False,
			CampaignLineSelectedKey = -1,
			CampaignColumnFocusKey = 0,
			LastScrollCampaignFocus = Null,
			FocusParentCampaign = False,
			Monthlies = [],
			IsLoadingMonthly = False,
			MonthlyColumnFocusKey = 0,
			LastScrollMonthlyFocus = Null,
			ScrollMonthlyOffset = 0,
			CurrentPageMonthly = -1,
			FocusParentMonthly = False,
			MonthlyLineSelectedKey = -1,
			Royals = [],
			IsLoadingRoyal = False,
			RoyalColumnFocusKey = 0,
			LastScrollRoyalFocus = Null,
			ScrollRoyalOffset = 0,
			CurrentPageRoyal = -1,
			FocusParentRoyal = False,
			RoyalLineSelectedKey = -1,
			CurrentMonthDays = []
		},
		Clubs = K_Clubs {
			Clubs = [],
			IsLoadingClubs = False,
			SelectedClub = ClubStruct::LibStructuresClub_K_Club {},
			IsLoadingCampaigns = False,
			SelectedCampaigns = [],
			FocusParentClub = False,
			SelectedClubKey = -1,
			IsLoadingCampaignTracks = False,
			FocusParentCampaign = False,
			SelectedCampaignKey = -1
		},
		SortingTypes = K_Sortings {
			IsFlatten = False,
			IsSortingByNameElseByDate = False,
			IsSortingFromAscendingOrder = False
		},
		Settings = K_Settings {
			ChosenOpeningTab = C_TabIndex_MyTracks,
			OpenOnLastTab = True,
			MultiSelect = False,
			ShowOnlyMyLocalTracks = False,
			IsBrowsingForEdition = False,
			ForceShowOfficialTracks = False
		},
		Filters = K_Filters {
			ShowOnlyUserTracks = False,
			ShowOnlyPlayableTracks = False,
			FilterByEnvironment = [EnvironmentInfo::C_Collection_Stadium],
			FilterByMapType = []
		},
		TracksFavoriteStatus = K_TracksFavoriteStatus {
			Request = Http::GetEmptyRequest(),
			CheckRequestTime = -1,
			LastAddOrRemoveRequestTime = -1,
			FirstHeartIconDisplay = False,
			UidsToCheck = [],
			KnownedFavoritesTracksUids = [],
			CurrentTrackUid = "",
			CurrentTrackName = ""
		},
		CanViewUGC = False
	};

	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global = (_This.Page.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameGlobal) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameTabs) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_SubTitle = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_LabelSubtitle) as CMlLabel);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_SectionTitle = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_LabelSectionTitle) as CMlLabel);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameLoadingSpinner) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameScrollTracks) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_AddTracks = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonAddSelectedTracks) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.ButtonIcon_AddTracks = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonIconAddTracks) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonBack) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_NoTracks = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_LabelNoTracks) as CMlLabel);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_NoTracksDetails = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_LabelNoTracksDetails) as CMlLabel);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_Error = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_LabelError) as CMlLabel);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MyTracks = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameMyTracks) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_MyLocalTracks = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MyTracks.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonMyLocalTracks) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_MyOnlineTracks = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MyTracks.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonMyOnlineTracks) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Official = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameOfficial) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_OfficialButtons = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameButtons) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_OfficialCampaigns = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_OfficialButtons.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonOfficialCampaigns) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_TOTD = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_OfficialButtons.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonTOTD) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_DayTOTD = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_OfficialButtons.GetFirstChild(C_Id_LabelTOTDDay) as CMlLabel);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Royal = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_OfficialButtons.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameRoyal) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Royal = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_OfficialButtons.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonRoyal) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_RoyalVictory = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_OfficialButtons.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameRoyalVictory) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Official_Campaigns = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Official.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameScrollOfficialCampaigns) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_TOTD = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Official.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameScrollTOTD) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Clubs = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameClubs) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Clubs = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Clubs.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameScrollClubs) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Options = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameOptions) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Options.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonSelectAllTracks) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.ButtonIcon_SelectAll = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Options.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonIconSelectAll) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Flatten = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonFlatten) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Refresh = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Options.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonRefresh) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_OpenExplorer = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Options.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonOpenExplorer) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Sort = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Options.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonSort) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.ButtonIcon_Sort = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Options.GetFirstChild(C_Id_ButtonIconSort) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SortPopUp = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameSortPopUp) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SortOption1 = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_SortOption1) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SortOption2 = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_SortOption2) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameMultichoice) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SpaceDisk = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameSpaceDisk) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SpaceDiskLeft = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SpaceDisk.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameSpaceLeftOnDisk) as CMlFrame);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_SpaceDiskLeft = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SpaceDisk.GetFirstChild(C_Id_LabelSpaceLeftOnDisk) as CMlLabel);
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner_PopUp = (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.GetFirstChild(C_Id_FrameLoadingSpinnerPopUpMultichoice) as CMlFrame);

	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LastButtonFocused = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_MyLocalTracks;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Official.LastButtonFocused = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_OfficialCampaigns;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.LastOptionButtonFocused = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Sort;

	Checkbox::Check(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Flatten, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsFlatten);
	Checkbox::Check(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SortOption1, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingByNameElseByDate);
	Checkbox::Check(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SortOption2, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingFromAscendingOrder);
	InitializeBrowser(_This);
}

Void MainLoop(CMlScript _This) {
	declare K_State Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State for _This.Page = C_State_Null;

	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.PendingEvents = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.DelayedPendingEvents;
	Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.DelayedPendingEvents = [];

	if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Global.Visible) {

		// Space disk left for local tracks update
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SpaceDisk.Visible && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SpaceLeftOnDiskInKB != DataFileMgr.UserSave_AvailableSpace) {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SpaceLeftOnDiskInKB = DataFileMgr.UserSave_AvailableSpace;

			declare Integer SpaceUsedInMB = ML::Max(0, C_MaxSpaceAvailableOnConsoleInMB - ML::TruncInteger(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SpaceLeftOnDiskInKB / 1024.));
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Label_SpaceDiskLeft.Value = TL::Compose(C_Text_SpaceLeftOnDisk, ""^SpaceUsedInMB, ""^C_MaxSpaceAvailableOnConsoleInMB);

			declare Real Ratio = (SpaceUsedInMB * 1.0) / (C_MaxSpaceAvailableOnConsoleInMB * 1.0);
			ExpendableAsset::SetWidth(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SpaceDiskLeft, Ratio * C_SpaceOnDiskAssetWidth);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SpaceDiskLeft.Visible = Ratio > 0.;
		}

		// Check current tracks favorite status
		if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CheckRequestTime != -1 && Now > Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CheckRequestTime) {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.CheckRequestTime = -1;
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request = Http::DestroyAndCreate(
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request,
				MapAPI::GetMaps(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.UidsToCheck, True)
			);
		}

		// Check UGC privilege
		if (
			!Privileges::Check_IsComplete(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.UGCPrivilegeCheck) &&
			!LoadingSpinner::IsLoading(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner)
		) {
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.UGCPrivilegeCheck = Privileges::Check_Update(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.UGCPrivilegeCheck);
			if (Privileges::Check_IsComplete(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.UGCPrivilegeCheck)) {
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CanViewUGC = Privileges::Check_HasPrivilege(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.UGCPrivilegeCheck);
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.UGCPrivilegeCheck = Privileges::Check_Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.UGCPrivilegeCheck);
				UpdateNavigationTabs(_This);
				if (!NavigationTabs::IsAvailableTab(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex)) {
					if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.ShowOnlyMyLocalTracks) {
						GoToTabAndSection(_This, C_TabIndex_MyTracks, C_Section_LocalTracks);
					} else {
						GoToTab(_This, C_TabIndex_MyTracks);
					}
				} else {
					Private_UpateTOTDAndRoyalAccess(_This, True);
				}
			}
		}

		/* Events PopUpBackground */
		foreach (Event in PopUpBackground::GetPendingEvents(_This)) {
			if (
				Event.Type == PopUpBackground::C_EventType_Close &&
				Event.PopUpBackground != Null &&
				Event.PopUpBackground.ControlId == C_Id_PopUpBackground &&
				!LoadingSpinner::IsLoading(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner)
			) {
				Display(_This, False);
			}
		}

		/* Events Navigation */
		foreach (Event in Navigation::GetPendingEvents(_This)) {
			if (Navigation::IsEventFromGroup(_This, Event, C_NavGroupName)) {
				switch (Event.Type) {
					case Navigation::C_EventType_NavigateInput: {
						if (Event.Input == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Select) {
							Select(_This, Event.To);
						} else if (Event.Input == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Cancel) {
							Cancel(_This);
						} else {
							Focus(_This, Event.From, Event.To);
						}
					}
					case Navigation::C_EventType_NavigateMouse: {
						if (Event.Mouse == CMlScriptEvent::Type::MouseClick) {
							Select(_This, Event.To);
						} else if (Event.Mouse == CMlScriptEvent::Type::MouseOver) {
							Focus(_This, Event.From, Event.To);
						}
					}
				}
			} else if (Navigation::IsEventFromGroup(_This, Event, C_NavGroupGlobal)) {
				if (Event.Input == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Action4 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Sort.Visible) {
					Select(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Sort);
				} else if (Event.Input == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Action3 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll.Visible) {
					if (Now > Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.LastSelectAllInputTime + C_DelayBetweenInput) {
						Select(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll);
						Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.LastSelectAllInputTime = Now;
					}
				} else if (Event.Input == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::AppMenu && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_AddTracks.Visible) {
					Select(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_AddTracks);
				}
			} else if (Navigation::IsEventFromGroup(_This, Event, PopUpMultiChoice::C_NavGroup)) {
				switch (Event.Type) {
					case Navigation::C_EventType_NavigateInput: {
						if (Event.Input == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Select) {
							Select(_This, Event.To);
						} else if ( // Can toggle the switch with right and left input
							(Event.Input == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Left || Event.Input == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Right) &&
							(Event.From.ControlId == Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SortOption1.ControlId || Event.From.ControlId == Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SortOption2.ControlId)
						) {
							if (
								(Event.Input == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Left && Checkbox::IsChecked(Event.From)) ||
								(Event.Input == CMlScriptEvent::EMenuNavAction::Right && !Checkbox::IsChecked(Event.From))
							) {
								Select(_This, Event.From);
							}
						}
					}
					case Navigation::C_EventType_NavigateMouse: {
						if (Event.Mouse == CMlScriptEvent::Type::MouseClick) {
							Select(_This, Event.To);
						} else if (Event.Mouse == CMlScriptEvent::Type::MouseOver) {
							Focus(_This, Event.From, Event.To);
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		/* Pop up multi choice events */
		foreach (Event in PopUpMultiChoice::GetPendingEvents(_This)) {
			if (Event.PopUpMultiChoice != Null) {
				if (Event.PopUpMultiChoice.Id == Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SortPopUp.Id) {
					switch (Event.Type) {
						case PopUpMultiChoice::C_EventType_Select: {
							if (Event.SelectedIndex == C_SortTracksPopUp_ChoiceIndex_Ok) {
								PopUpMultiChoice::Close(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SortPopUp, True);
							}
						}
						case PopUpMultiChoice::C_EventType_Display: {
							LockBrowser(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SortPopUp.Visible);
							if (
								!Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_SortPopUp.Visible &&
								(
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingByNameElseByDate != Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.LastIsSortingByNameElseByDate ||
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingFromAscendingOrder != Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.LastIsSortingFromAscendingOrder
								)
							) {
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.LastIsSortingByNameElseByDate = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingByNameElseByDate;
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.LastIsSortingFromAscendingOrder = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SortingTypes.IsSortingFromAscendingOrder;
								Refresh(_This);
							}
						}
					}
				} else if (Event.PopUpMultiChoice.Id == Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice.Id) {
					switch (Event.Type) {
						case PopUpMultiChoice::C_EventType_Select: {
							declare Integer PopUpType for Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice;
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks) {
								if (Event.SelectedIndex == C_DeleteTrackPopUp_ChoiceIndex_Delete && PopUpType == C_PopUpDeleteTrackIndex && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.FileName != "") {
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task = Task::DestroyAndCreate(
										Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task,
										DataFileMgr,
										DataFileMgr.UserSave_DeleteFile("Maps/"^Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.FileName)
									);
								} else if (PopUpType == C_PopUpUploadTrackIndex) {
									if (Event.SelectedIndex == C_UploadTrackPopUp_ChoiceIndex_Upload && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Uid != "") {
										Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task = Task::DestroyAndCreate(
											Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task,
											DataFileMgr,
											DataFileMgr.Map_NadeoServices_Register(MainUser::GetMainUserId(), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Uid)
										);
										SetLoadingSpinnerPopUp(_This, True, C_Text_UploadingTrackOnline);
									} else if (Event.SelectedIndex == C_UploadTrackPopUp_ChoiceIndex_Back) {
										PopUpMultiChoice::Close(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice);
									}
								}
							} else if (
								Event.SelectedIndex == C_RemoveFavoriteMapPopUp_ChoiceIndex_Remove &&
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Favorites &&
								PopUpType == C_PopUpRemoveFavoriteTrackIndex &&
								Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.RemoveTrack.Uid != ""
							) {
								MapStore::Action_RemoveMapFromFavorites(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Favorites.RemoveTrack.Uid);
							}
						}
						case PopUpMultiChoice::C_EventType_Display: {
							if (!Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice.Visible && LoadingSpinner::IsLoading(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner_PopUp)) {
								LoadingSpinner::SetIsLoading(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner_PopUp, False);
							}
							LockBrowser(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice.Visible);
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		/* Scroll events */
		Private_ProcessScrollEvents(_This);

		/* Special mouse events */
		foreach (Event in _This.PendingEvents) {
			switch (Event.Type) {
				case CMlScriptEvent::Type::MouseOver: {
					if (Event.Control != Null) {
						if (Event.Control.Parent.Parent != Null) {
							if (Event.Control.HasClass(C_Class_OfficialCampaign_Mouse_Navigation)) {
								FocusOfficialCampaignByMouse(_This, Event.Control.Parent.Parent);
							}	else if (Event.Control.HasClass(C_Class_Monthly_Mouse_Navigation)) {
								FocusMonthlyByMouse(_This, Event.Control.Parent.Parent, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal);
							}
						}
						if (Event.Control.HasClass(C_Class_TrackOptions_Mouse_Navigation)) {
							MenuSounds::PlaySound(_This, MenuSounds::C_Sound_Focus);
							_This.AnimMgr.Flush(Event.Control);
							_This.AnimMgr.Add(Event.Control, "<anim opacity=\"1.\" scale=\"1.2\"/>", 200, CAnimManager::EAnimManagerEasing::QuadOut);
						}
					}
				}
				case CMlScriptEvent::Type::MouseOut: {
					if (Event.Control != Null && Event.Control.HasClass(C_Class_TrackOptions_Mouse_Navigation)) {
						_This.AnimMgr.Flush(Event.Control);
						_This.AnimMgr.Add(Event.Control, "<anim opacity=\"0.7\" scale=\"1.\"/>", 200, CAnimManager::EAnimManagerEasing::QuadOut);
					}
				}
				case CMlScriptEvent::Type::MouseClick: {
					if (Event.Control.Parent.Parent.Parent != Null) {
						if (Event.Control.HasClass(C_Class_OfficialCampaign_Mouse_Navigation)) {
							assert(Event.Control.Parent.Parent.Parent.HasClass(Scroll::C_Class_Element), "We are not pointing to the correct frame anymore");
							declare Integer CampaignScrollKey for Event.Control.Parent.Parent.Parent;
							SelectOfficialCampaign(_This, CampaignScrollKey);
						} else if (Event.Control.HasClass(C_Class_Monthly_Mouse_Navigation)) {
							assert(Event.Control.Parent.Parent.Parent.HasClass(Scroll::C_Class_Element), "We are not pointing to the correct frame anymore");
							declare Integer MonthlyScrollKey for Event.Control.Parent.Parent.Parent;
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Monthly) SelectMonthly(_This, MonthlyScrollKey);
							else if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_Royal) SelectRoyal(_This, MonthlyScrollKey);
						}
					}
					if (Event.Control.Parent.Parent != Null) {
						if (Event.Control.HasClass(C_Class_TrackOptions_Mouse_Navigation)) {
							assert(Event.Control.Parent.Parent.HasClass(Scroll::C_Class_Element), "We are not pointing to the correct frame anymore");
							MenuSounds::PlaySound(_This, MenuSounds::C_Sound_Select);
							if (Event.ControlId == C_Id_ButtonDeleteMyTrack) {
								declare Integer TrackScrollKey for Event.Control.Parent.Parent;
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks && !Task::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task)) {
									OpenPopUp_DeleteLocalTrack(_This, TrackScrollKey);
								}
							} else if (Event.ControlId == C_Id_ButtonUploadMyTrack) {
								declare Integer TrackScrollKey for Event.Control.Parent.Parent;
								if (
									Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentSection == C_Section_LocalTracks &&
									!Task::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus) &&
									!Task::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task)
								) {
									OpenPopUp_UploadLocalTrack(_This, TrackScrollKey);
								}
							} else if (Event.ControlId == C_Id_ButtonRemoveTrackFromFavorites) {
								declare Integer TrackScrollKey for Event.Control.Parent.Parent;
								if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex == C_TabIndex_Favorites) {
									OpenPopUp_RemoveFavoriteTrack(_This, TrackScrollKey);
								}
							} else if (Event.ControlId == C_Id_ButtonFavorite) {
								declare Integer TrackScrollKey for Event.Control.Parent.Parent;
								AddOrRemoveFocusedTrackToFavorites(_This, TrackScrollKey);
							}
						} else if (Event.ControlId == C_Id_ButtonCheckboxTrack) {
							assert(Event.Control.Parent.HasClass(Scroll::C_Class_Element), "We are not pointing to the correct frame anymore");
							declare Integer TrackScrollKey for Event.Control.Parent;
							if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect) {
								AddTrackToSelection(_This, TrackScrollKey, Event.Control.Parent);
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		/* Events NavigationTabs */
		foreach (Event in NavigationTabs::GetPendingEvents(_This)) {
			switch (Event.Type) {
				case NavigationTabs::C_EventType_Select: {
					if (Event.Frame_NavigationTabs.ControlId == Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs.ControlId) {
						// Check this condition for the rare case of the player clicking on both a tab and en element to load (example : an official campaign)
						if (!LoadingSpinner::IsLoading(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_LoadingSpinner) && !Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.ShowOnlyMyLocalTracks) {
							GoToTab(_This, Event.CurrentTab);
						}	else if (Event.CurrentTab != Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex) {
							NavigationTabs::UpdateCurrentTab(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.CurrentTabIndex, False);
						}
					}

					// Text to speech context
					Private_GetParentApp(_This).TTS_Context_Change(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TTSContextIdent_Tabs, NavigationTabs::GetCurrentTabLabel(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Tabs));
					Private_GetParentApp(_This).TTS_Context_Read(TextToSpeech::C_ContextLevel_Component);
				}
			}
		}

		/* Store events */
		Private_ProcessStoreEvents(_This);
	}

	// Local tracks task
	if (Task::IsInitialized(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetLocalTracks)) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetLocalTracks = Task::Update(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetLocalTracks);
		if (!Task::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetLocalTracks)) {
			declare CTaskResult_MapList SourceTask = Task::GetSourceTask_MapList(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetLocalTracks);
			if (Task::IsSuccess(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetLocalTracks) && SourceTask != Null) {
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.clear();
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentPath = SourceTask.Path;
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentParentPath = SourceTask.ParentPath;

				declare CurrentPath = TL::Replace(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.CurrentPath, "\\", "/");
				if (TL::EndsWith("/", CurrentPath)) CurrentPath = TL::SubString(CurrentPath, 0, TL::Length(CurrentPath)-1);
				if (CurrentPath != "" && Platform::IsPC(System)) SetSectionTitle(_This, TL::Compose("%1%2%3", C_Text_LocalTracks, "/", FilterProfanities(CurrentPath)));
				else SetSectionTitle(_This, C_Text_LocalTracks);

				foreach (SubFolder in SourceTask.SubFolders) {
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.add(K_LocalTrack {
						ParentPath = SourceTask.ParentPath,
						Path = SourceTask.Path,
						TrackInfo = CampaignStruct::LibCampaignStruct_K_Map {},
						SubFolder = SubFolder
					});
				}

				declare Boolean NeedFilter = TracksShouldBeFiltered(_This);
				foreach (TrackInfo in SourceTask.MapInfos) {
					declare CampaignStruct::LibCampaignStruct_K_Map Map = CampaignStruct::GetMapFromMapInfo(TrackInfo);
					// Local maps are made by the current player, so AuthorIsFirstPartyDisplayName is always True on consoles
					Map.AuthorIsFirstPartyDisplayName = Platform::IsFromFirstParty(System);
					if (!NeedFilter || FilterTrack(_This, Map.AuthorLogin, Map.IsPlayable, Map.CollectionName, Map.Type)) {
						Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.add(K_LocalTrack {
							ParentPath = SourceTask.ParentPath,
							Path = SourceTask.Path,
							TrackInfo = Map,
							SubFolder = ""
						});
					}
				}

				// Hide SelectAllTracks button when not usable
				if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect) {
					declare Boolean OnlyFolders = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.count == SourceTask.SubFolders.count;
					EnableOption(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_SelectAll, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect && !OnlyFolders);
				}

				Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LocalTracks.count);
				if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LastFolderSelected_Keys.count > 0 && Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.FocusParentFolder) {
					Scroll::ScrollToElement(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LastFolderSelected_Keys[Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LastFolderSelected_Keys.count-1], True);
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LastFolderSelected_Keys.removekey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.LastFolderSelected_Keys.count-1);
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.FocusParentFolder = False;
				}
			} else if (SourceTask != Null) {
				//L16N Error while retrieving player's local tracks. %1 will be replaced with a code e.g. "Error code: 500"
				ShowError(_This, TL::Compose(_("Error while retrieving your local tracks. (Error code: %1)"), SourceTask.ErrorCode));
				Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
			}
			UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetLocalTracks = Task::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetLocalTracks);
		}
	}

	// Online tracks task
	if (Task::IsInitialized(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetOnlineTracks)) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetOnlineTracks = Task::Update(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetOnlineTracks);
		if (!Task::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetOnlineTracks)) {
			declare CTaskResult_NSMapList SourceTask = Task::GetSourceTask_NSMapList(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetOnlineTracks);
			if (Task::IsSuccess(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetOnlineTracks) && SourceTask != Null) {
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks.clear();
				SetSectionTitle(_This, C_Text_OnlineTracks);

				declare Boolean NeedFilter = TracksShouldBeFiltered(_This);
				declare Integer Index = 0;
				foreach (NSMap in SourceTask.MapList) {
					declare CampaignStruct::LibCampaignStruct_K_Map Map = CampaignStruct::GetMapFromNSMap(CampaignStruct::LibCampaignStruct_K_Map {}, NSMap);
					if (!NeedFilter || FilterTrack(_This, Map.AuthorLogin, Map.IsPlayable, Map.CollectionName, Map.Type)) {
						Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks[Index] = Map;
						Index += 1;
					}
				}
				Scroll::SetElementsTotal(_This, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks, Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks.count);
				CheckTracksFavoriteStatus(_This);
			} else if (SourceTask != Null) {
				//L16N Error while retrieving player's online tracks. %1 will be replaced with a code e.g. "Error code: 500"
				ShowError(_This, TL::Compose(_("Error while retrieving your online tracks. (Error code: %1)"), SourceTask.ErrorCode));
				Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Button_Back);
			}
			UpdateLoadingStatus(_This);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetOnlineTracks = Task::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_GetOnlineTracks);
		}
	}

	// Check all tracks favorite status
	if (Http::IsInitialized(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request)) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request = Http::Update(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request);
		if (!Http::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request)) {
			if (Http::IsSuccess(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request)) {
				declare Response = MapAPI::GetResponseFromGetMaps(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request);
				foreach (I => Track in Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks) {
					if (Response.Maps.existskey(Track.Uid) && Response.Maps[Track.Uid].IsFavorite) {
						Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.KnownedFavoritesTracksUids.add(Track.Uid);
					}
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Tracks[I].IsFavorite = Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.KnownedFavoritesTracksUids.exists(Track.Uid);
				}
				Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.FirstHeartIconDisplay = True;
