				Focus(_This, Navigation::GetFocusedControl(_This, C_NavGroupName), Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_Scroll_Tracks);
			}
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request = Http::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.TracksFavoriteStatus.Request);
		}
	}

	// Check track status task
	if (Task::IsInitialized(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus)) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus = Task::Update(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus);
		if (!Task::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus)) {
			declare CTaskResult_NSMap SourceTask = Task::GetSourceTask_NSMap(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus);

			declare Text NewDescriptionDeleteTrack = C_DeleteTrackPopUp_Description2;
			declare Vec3 NewColorDescriptionDeleteTrack = Stylesheet::GetColorRGB(Stylesheet::C_Color_AccentOne);
			declare Integer PopUpType for Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice;

			if (Task::IsSuccess(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus) && SourceTask != Null && SourceTask.Map != Null) {
				if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice.Visible) {
					if (PopUpType == C_PopUpDeleteTrackIndex && (SourceTask.Map.SubmitterWebServicesUserId == LocalUser.WebServicesUserId)) {
						NewDescriptionDeleteTrack = C_DeleteTrackPopUp_Description3;
						NewColorDescriptionDeleteTrack = <1., 1., 1.>;
					} else if (PopUpType == C_PopUpUploadTrackIndex) {
						EditUploadLocalTrackPopUp(_This, True, False, True, (SourceTask.Map.SubmitterWebServicesUserId == LocalUser.WebServicesUserId), False, "");
					}
				}
			} else {
				if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice.Visible) {
					if (PopUpType == C_PopUpUploadTrackIndex) {
						EditUploadLocalTrackPopUp(_This, True, False, False, False, False, "");
					}
				}
			}

			if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice.Visible && PopUpType == C_PopUpDeleteTrackIndex) {
				PopUpMultiChoice::SetDescription(
					_This,
					Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Controls.Frame_MultiChoice,
					[
						PopUpMultiChoice::CreateDescriptionPart(TL::Compose(C_DeleteTrackPopUp_Description1, "$<"^Tools::FormatValue(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Name)^"$>"), <130., 15.>, 3., Stylesheet::GetFont(Stylesheet::C_Font_Weight_Regular), "$t$i", <1., 1., 1.>, False),
						PopUpMultiChoice::CreateDescriptionPart(NewDescriptionDeleteTrack, <130., 10.>, 3., Stylesheet::GetFont(Stylesheet::C_Font_Weight_SemiBold), "$t$i", NewColorDescriptionDeleteTrack, False)
					],
					True
				);
			}
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus = Task::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.Task_CheckTrackUploadStatus);
		}
	}

	// Delete local track task
	if (Task::IsInitialized(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task)) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task = Task::Update(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task);
		if (!Task::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task)) {
			declare CTaskResult SourceTask = Task::GetSourceTask(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task);
			if (Task::IsSuccess(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task)) {
				// Remove track from selected tracks if necessary
				if (Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.Settings.MultiSelect) Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.SelectedTracks.removekey(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Uid);
				Refresh(_This);
			} else {
				declare Text ErrorCode = Error::C_Code_TrackBrowser_DeleteTrackTaskNull;
				if (SourceTask != Null) {
					ErrorCode = SourceTask.ErrorCode;
				}
				//L16N Error while deleting a local track. %1 will be replaced by the track name and %2 will be replaced with a code e.g. "Error while deleting the local track 'Test 2'. (Error code: 500)"
				ShowError(_This, TL::Compose(_("Error while deleting the local track '%1'. (Error code: %2)"), "$<"^Tools::FormatValue(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Name)^"$>", ErrorCode));
			}
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task = Task::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Task);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Name = "";
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.FileName = "";
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.DeleteLocalTrack.Uid = "";
		}
	}

	// Upload local track task
	if (Task::IsInitialized(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task)) {
		Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task = Task::Update(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task);
		if (!Task::IsRunning(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task)) {
			if (Task::IsSuccess(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task)) {
				EditUploadLocalTrackPopUp(_This, False, False, False, False, True, "");
			} else {
				EditUploadLocalTrackPopUp(_This, False, False, False, False, True, Task::GetSourceTaskError(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task).Code);
			}
			SetLoadingSpinnerPopUp(_This, False, "");
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task = Task::Destroy(Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Task);
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Name = "";
			Trackmania_TrackBrowser_State.MyTracks.UploadLocalTrack.Uid = "";
		}
	}
}

// ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~ //

 *
 *	@return														The component id
 */
Text ComponentV2() {
	return MV::ComponentV2(
		C_Name,
		GetManialink(),
"""
#Include "Libs/Nadeo/Trackmania/Components/TrackBrowser.Script.txt" as {{{Q}}}
""",
"""
***MainInit***
***
{{{P}}}MainInit(This);
***

***MainStart***
***
{{{P}}}MainStart(This);
***

***MainLoop***
***
{{{P}}}MainLoop(This);
***
""",
[
	Transition::ComponentV2(),
	PopUpBackground::ComponentV2(),
	Navigation::ComponentV2(),
	ExpendableButton_Trackmania::ComponentV2(),
	ButtonIcon::ComponentV2(),
	Button::ComponentV2(),
	NavigationTabs::ComponentV2(),
	Scroll::ComponentV2(),
	CampaignStruct::Component(),
	LoadingSpinner::ComponentV2(),
	UserStore::ComponentV2(),
	MapStore::ComponentV2(),
	ClubStore::ComponentV2(),
	ClubStruct::Component(),
	CampaignStore::ComponentV2(),
	MenuSounds::ComponentV2(),
	PopUpMultiChoice::ComponentV2(),
	Checkbox::ComponentV2(),
	Router::ComponentV2(),
	ExpendableAsset_Trackmania::ComponentV2(),
	PlayerRoyalVictories::ComponentV2(),
	PlayerName::ComponentV2(),
	ControlBlockList::ComponentV2()
],
[]
);
}
